saṃhitāyām śrī gaṇeśāya namaḥ prapadyet evam ayam śānam sarvajñam aparājitam sambhavam sarva bhūtānām anādi viśvatomukham veda ādau yaḥ svaraḥ proktaḥ oṃkāra ākhyaḥ maheśvaraḥ sṛjate sarva bhūtāni pañcabhūtaiḥ sadāśivaḥ sāṃkhyānām paramam yogam vrataiḥ pāśupataiḥ tathā rakṣā arthaiḥ sarva jantūnām tridhā ātmānam sṛjati ajaḥ sa saṃjñayā tu bhagavant ekaḥ eva maheśvaraḥ mahā śūlam ghora rūpam mahā aśanim nānā krīḍanakaiḥ devaḥ krīḍate yoga māyayā dayitā ardha vapus rutvā nṛtya ārambhe sthitaḥ haraḥ tad bhaktyā saṃpravakṣyāmi purāṇam śiva bhāṣitam parāśarasya dāyādaḥ śrīmān satyavatī sutaḥ brahmarṣiḥ saca dharma ātma akāla yoga vidām varaḥ ṛṣi saṃdhaiḥ parivṛtaḥ śrutaiḥ iva pitāmahaḥ bhārate śatasāhakhyām saṃhitāyām kavi īśvaraḥ caturdhā avyasya matimān iiśaṣyān ca adhyāpayat pṛthak teṣām sukha upaviṣṭānām kathām kathayatām parām tatra ca adhyātma dharma ātma brahmanaḥ tanayaḥ śubhaḥ anugraha artham ṭaṣīṇām darśanam kṛtavan ṛṣiḥ sadadarśa sukha āsīnān brahmarṣīn amita ojasaḥ teṣām dattam ca dharma vid tatas saṃpūjayāmāsa valapīn saṃśita vratān anujñātaḥ ca taiḥ sarvaiḥ upaviṣṭaḥ kuśa āsane pṛṣṭaḥ tu ṛṣibhiḥ tatratra hma putraḥ mahā muniḥ tasya cayat puṇyam devadevasya dhīmataḥ mūrtīnām tu vibhāgasya mantrasya paramam vidhim sthānān iti aṣṭa asya api rudrasya tu mahātmanaḥ upaviṣṭaiḥ tu bhagavant yogi īśaḥ brahmanaḥ sutaḥ tapaḥ veṣa anurūpeṣu āsaneṣu yathāyatham mad sanatkumārasaṃhitā vivṛtau prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ om om namaḥ śivāya atha dvitīye ṛṣibhiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ brahma sutaḥ bravīt pāvanam śraddadhānānām iha loke paratra ca prakṛtyā artha adhikāreṇa pradhāna purupa īśvara purāṇam śiva bhāpitam hrutam purā mayā vyāsāt devadevasya dhīmataḥ yat aham tat pravakṣyāmi yathā pūrva śrutam mayā saṃkṣepāt ca eva vakṣyāmi pṛthivī ādi yathā tathā saptadvīpasya ca ākhyānam varṣāṇām ca tathā eva ca sanatkumāra vikāntam rudrasya vihitam kṛtam mahādevam brahmanaḥ tanayena tu vara dānena sambandhaḥ muni śiṣya samāgamaḥ bhavanam meru śṛṅgasya brahma viṣṇu maheśvarān bhīṣaṇasya saṃvādam rudrasya ca mahātmanaḥ sarva tīrtha phalam puṇyam śiva liṅgasya pūjanam liṅga arcana vidhim ca eva devasya pūjanam tathā prāsādasya ca yat puṇyam mahādevasya dhīmataḥ sthāna ādi jyaiṣṭhyam asya api rūpasya tu mahātmanaḥ liṅga saṃsthāpane puṇyam puṣpa dānasya yat phalam dhūpasya ca vidhim ca eva māsānām ca param phalam yathā dvādaśa jyotis liś ādīnām caturdaśyām atha aṣṭamyām vidhāne vihite phalam ca tathā vailakṣaṇya aṣṭamīm yoganāḍyāḥ tathā ākhyānam mayā a proktam purātanam avimuktasya māhātmyam tathā ca oṃkāra varṇanam yajñeśvarasya māhātmyam tathā tīrtha anuvarṇanam bhagavat ārādhanam nandeḥ tathā anaṃya bhiṣecanam nīlakaṇṭhasya māhātmyam tripurasya tathā avadhaḥ vāsudevasya māhātmyam vidhānam ca eva tasya ca mokṣam parama saṃpadam idānīm vistaram citram vibhāgam rūpam aiśvaram āsīt tamaḥ mayam sarvam aprajñātam alakṣaṇam ātmanā sarvam ātmānam saṃcintya bhagavant haraḥ manaḥ saṃsṛjate pūrvam ahaṃkāram tu pṛṣṭhatas ahaṃkārāt prajātāni mahābhūtāni paṃca ca aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ proktāḥ vikārāḥ ca eva ṣoḍaśa hastaḥ sparśaḥ ca rūpam ca rasaḥ gandhaḥ tathā eva ca prāṇa upānaḥ samāna śvaidānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca sattvam rajaḥ tamaḥ ca eva guṇāḥ proktāḥ tu te trayaḥ tasmāt bhagavantaḥ brahmā a tasmāt viṣṇuḥ ajāyata tasmāt parataram na asti na asti tasmāt param śivam brahma a viṣṇu śrva dvau etau udbhūtau śaṃkara ā ttutau tapasā āharate ca eva nānā bhūtāni sarvaśas hi dina ekam brahmanaḥ proktam niśā kalpaḥ tathā ācyate evam māsam ca varṣam ca tathā varṣa śatam dvijāḥ evamādi parārdhī taḥ harasi ani miṣaḥ smṛtaḥ brahma ādi stamba paryantam nimiṣaḥ ca maheśvaraḥ sarva candra ādīnām grahaiḥ saha pātālam sutalam tālam vitalam talam eva ca pañcamam viddhi pātālam rukma sauvarṇikam smṛtam saptamam śarkarābhūmiḥ aṣṭamam vijayam smṛtam aṣṭaupātālavāsinaḥ ante rudraḥ prakīrtitaḥ evam prakurute lokān krīḍā artham tu maheśvaraḥ brahmaloka parīmāṇa gatiḥ ūrdhva vivarṇitā pṛthi ca antarikṣam ca diśa śru avidiśaḥ tathā samuccaya ṃgirīṇām ca anukramaṇa saṃkhyayā samudrāṇām ca vistāram pramāṇam ca tathā śṭaṇu sthāvarāṇām carāṇām ca devānām ca divaukasām catuṣpāda dvipādānām dhārmikān karma mokṣakān sahasraguṇam ākhyātam sthāvarāṇām prakīrtitam tat saha sampāda hīna aśvāḥ iti āha bhagavant śivaḥ maheśvaraḥ paraḥ teṣām sarveṣām deva mānuṣāt evam saṃkhyā atra saṃkhyātā sarvajñena svayambhunā anyeṣām māheśvaram jñānam bhakti mantraiḥ prakīrtitam ekam jñānam namasyaṃti abhūtam bhūta saṃjñakam nirguṇam nirmalam jñānam śaṃkareṇa pracoditam ṛṣīṇām śrotu kāmānām bhaktānām ca dṛḍha vrata mad sarva svam purāṇeṣu ca gīyate tatas jñānam param śreṣṭhaiḥ proktam īśena dhīmatā brāhmaṇānām hita arthāya sarva varṇe viśeṣataḥ yathā saṃbhavati jñānam tathā īśaḥ pravartate mad mad ādi śva madhyam ca aham ca te ca saṃsthitaḥ tam īhate vyāsaḥ utpannamatiḥ avyayaḥ tatas kālaḥ hi bhagavant saḥ abhidhyāya śiva ājñayā kurvan prakṛti nāma nāmnaḥ tasmāt brahmā apraka tyā astu utpannaḥ saha viṣṇunā pāda hīnān kṣaciyān śvan a tasmāt hīnān tu vaiśyaiḥ kān caturtha pāda hīna aṃśvaḥ ācāraiḥ avahiṣkṛtān makalpayat tathā lokālokasya saṃkhyānam dvipadām uddheḥ tathā saritām sāgarāṇām ca tīrthāni āyatanāni ca ulkānipātam ketum ca jyotiṣāṃpatanāni api evam sarva artha saṣṭāvai codyamānaḥ śivena vai utpannam ca eva tat sarvam bhūyas kālena pīḍyate ca katham brahmā asamutpannaḥ katham sṛṣṭiḥ pravartate jñāyata tamaḥ mayam ca etat na prājñāyata kiṃcana tatas śivaḥ mahādevaḥ yogadhṛk satu sarvaśas tasmāt pṛthvī tvam āpannam tasmāt apaḥ tatobhuvaḥ tat tamaḥ udārayāmāsa āpaḥ bhūtvā tu śaṃkaraḥ tasmāt tu teja sā ca eva vāyunā ca sadā ākṣipan tasmāt aṇḍa samutpattiḥ tatas nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ apāṃcāgneya asaṃyogāt agniḥ tejas śvasambhavaḥ vāyoḥ apivikurvāṇāt ākāśam abhavat tadā tathā abhavat pṛthvī eṣām māheśvarī tanuḥ atra praviśya hi jalam nimiṣa ardha pramāṇāt tatas brahmā samutpannaḥ adbhiḥ nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ bhagavān uṣitvā aparivatsarān tatas vaibrāhmaṇaḥ jajñe kāle kālena coditaḥ atha vyoma diśa śva aṣṭa apām sthānam ca śāśvatam tatas sakālam adhyetu saḥ atha sṛṣṭim atha akarot iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumāra saṃhitāyām tṛtīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ mahantaḥ tu tatas brahmā tasmāt rahmāṇḍa tām gataḥ tasya rudhiram ākāśam udaram tathā pavanaḥ ca eva niḥśvāsaḥ tejas nirnimnagā rasaḥ ākāśa tamasī śrotre candra arkau nayanau smṛtau pṛthivī ante samudra aśva samudra ante tamaḥ smṛtam adhipāḥ tad aṃte punar ākāśam tasya api aṃte punar jalam aṇḍasya dhāraṇāt sadma mahat aśva mahātmanaḥ evam brahmāṇḍam iti uktam mahā dhāraṇam ucyate yaḥ yathā yasya yoni tva etam pravakṣyāmi aśeṣatas mad apaḥ nareṇavaiḥ sṛṣṭāḥ āpaḥ vai nara sū navaḥ tāyat asya ayanam pūrvatena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ tad ālokāḥ tatas jīvāḥ sattvāḥ pañca ātmakāḥ smṛtāḥ caturvidhāḥ ṣṭavidhā devayoniḥ mānuṣāḥ tu ekavidhayā mānuṣyam ca ekavidham tu cāturvarṇyam anekadhā pṛthivī ca antarikṣam ca tri divam bhuvanam smṛtam pṛthivyāḥ tu parīmāṇe bhūyas tulyaḥ vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ekam tu koṭyā vikhyātam evam tribhuvanam matam rudrāṇām koṭiḥ ekātu pure ca antar vyavasthitā maheśvaram pṛthivī ādi prasaṃkhyāna tapas a samudāhṛ tat idam saṃpravakṣyāmi puruṣān loka viśrutān śiva krīḍana saṃsthānam śive na parikalpitam kāma ārādhanakam śambhoḥ pūjanam dvīpa vāsibhiḥ sārdha pañcā śīti śata yojana ādi visāriṣu jambūdvīpa ādi dvīpa iṣu mayā vyāptam idam dvija haima dīpe mahādevaḥ gomedegirijeśvaraḥ śālmali dvīpa madhya sthā devaḥ paśupatiḥ svayam bhūtvā krauñce proktaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ mām yam puṣkara ibha alalocanaḥ tatra tatra mahādevam pūjayantaḥ sthirān abahūn bhogān mahā auṣadhīḥ tebhyaḥ prāpnuvanti śiva ājñayā yambūddīpaḥ ca gomeda śālmaliḥ ca kuśaḥ tathā bhauñcadvīpaḥ tathā śākaḥ puṣkaraḥ samamaḥ smṛtaḥ tatas param pravakṣyāmi dīpānām pṛthak pṛthak parimāṇam ca saṃkhyām ca dvīpa pravaram eva ca mambūdvīpe jambu vṛkṣaḥ yojanaiḥ tat nibodhata sahasram śatam ekam ca yojanānām samucchritaḥ tasya jambu phala rasaḥ ca amṛta svāduḥ ucyate tasya jambu phala rasaḥ ca amṛta svāduḥ ucyate pramāṇādāḥ yatas dvīpa udviguṇaḥ pariṇāhāt dviguṇena samudreṇa lavaṇena samāvṛtaḥ tasya varṣāṇi sa meha kāmagāḥ ca yathārhāt bhāratasya varṣasi anava bhedāḥ prakītitāḥ sapta vargāḥ prasaṃkhyātāḥ samā eva kulaparvatāḥ dakṣiṇena visam khyātam ilāvattam prakīrtitam uttaram dakṣiṇam ca eva indradhanva ākṛtiḥ yathā catvāraḥ droṇa saṃsthānām varṣāṇām ca pramāṇāt giri varṣaḥ kimpuruṣaḥ bhāratam dakṣiṇena tu pūrveṇa mālyavant ca eva paścime gandhamādanaḥ nīlaḥ parvatarāja śva śvetaḥ śuklaḥ mahā giriḥ mṛṅgāt uttaratas pārśve samantāt samupotthitau sahasrāṇām tasmin jambūdaka iti eva kanakam deva bhūṣaṇam tasya jambūttare pārśvameruḥ nāma mahā giriḥ merum pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā punar yojanānām sahasrāṇi caturaśītiḥ ucchrayaḥ adhastāt daśa sahasrāṇi viṃśaḥ ca eva pārśvatas merum pradakṣiṇam kṛtvā kailāsa ākhyaḥ tatas giriḥ caturaśītiḥ tatas vyāsaḥ giri indrasya mahātmanaḥ tasya sānuṣu citreṣu kandareṣu darīṣu ca tatra āyati jita krodha ajita lobha ajita indriyāḥ tatra āyati jita krodha ajita lobha ajita indriyāḥ ye gṛhasthāḥ svadharma jñāḥ gaḥ brāhmaṇa hite ratāḥ te yānti paramam sthānam prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ śatam śata sahasrāṇi yojanānām samaṃtataḥ mahā nīla vasu niṣadhaḥ ca eva hemakūṭaḥ ca parvataḥ himavant dakṣiṇe pārśve tāvat paramam ucchritaḥ pañcaviṃśat sahasrāṇi vistareṇa sadā ucyate tathā eva vakṣa sindhu śvati srastā vaipratīcya gāḥ ca eva pūrva gāḥ tāsām jambu div pasarit varā gaṅgā samāna rūpa aśrva puṇya tīrya śiloccayāḥ deva tīryāḥ su puṇya aśva pṛthivyām anukīrtitāḥ jambūdvīpaḥ prasaṃkhyātaḥ yāthātathyena vai dvijāḥ paṇṇām itara dvīpānām śeṣam prāmāṇyāt śṛṇu jambūdvīpa pramāṇena dviguṇa antarāt smṛtaḥ uttareṇa smṛtāḥ sarve antare svarga vāsinaḥ dvīpādvīpa samānasya nāmadheyāni sarvaśas tad ekṣuḥ surā sarpiḥ dadhi odān āma nāmnaḥ maṇḍodaḥ ca prasaṃkhyātaḥ tatas svādaka uttaraḥ dvīpānām sahasrāṇi tu dvijāḥ api varṣa śataiḥ viprān aśakyam kathitum mayā taḥ śālmale śālmaliḥ smṛtaḥ kuśadvīpe kuśaḥ tam vaḥ krauñcadvīpe mahā giriḥ mṛtaḥ sarveṣām eva vṛkṣāṇām amṛta svāduḥ ucyate tam tu pītvā amṭata rasam dīrgha āyuḥ stavam ca gacchati na anyam priyam vijānaṃti cakravāka sadharmiṇaḥ sūkṣma kāñcana vālukā sarva kālaphalā vṛkṣāḥ sva sva gandha phala āśrayāḥ sarve pāñca eva dvīpānām saptānām kulaparvatāḥ nadyaḥ teṣām tu samā eva kalpitāḥ śubhāḥ tāsām nadī upanadī astu śataśas utha sahasraśas teṣām parvata rājānam parivārya samaṃtataḥ raṃjitāḥ śṛṃgavantaḥ vaśobhate girayaḥ tathā tatas siddha aśva ṛṣayaḥ gandharvāḥ dānavāḥ khagāḥ aśivaḥ teṣām parvata jālāni dīpyanti prabhayā svayā vṛtāḥ parvata rājāḥ samaṃtataḥ ṣaṣṭiṃgiri sahasrāṇi ete tasya samam tadā tatra te puruṣāḥ divyāḥ śukla dantāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ teṣām na duḥkham na glāniḥ na kaścid paribādhate teṣu dvīpeṣu jāyaṃte puruṣāḥ te tapodhanāḥ dīrgha āyuṣvaṃtam teṣām vidyate kāmagā gatiḥ jambūdvīpasya paryāyam kathayiṣyāmi vai dvijāḥ mānuṣāṇām ca varṣāṇi yugānām ca eva saṃkhyayā purāṇam yat vibhāvyate viduḥ lakṣāḥ dvādaśa vaipra uktāḥ ṣaṣ sahasrāṇi vatsarāḥ tretā yugasya prāmāṇyam purāṇe parikīrtitam tad aṣṭa varṣa sahasra anta alakṣa aśva aṣṭa prakīrtitāḥ tathā aśva aṣṭa cala kṣaudyau ayuta idva tayā eva ca aṣṭa varṣa sahasrati kālaḥ evamādi ca varṣa ca tathā varṣa śatam dvijāḥ evam āyus jita indrasya harasya animiṣaḥ smṛtaḥ brahma ādi stamba paryantam nimiṣa utpattiḥ īśvaraḥ nimeṣa jīvinaḥ sarve candra ādityau gṛhaiḥ saha mahākalpam ca vikhyātam śivasya nimiṣaḥ tathā dvīpānām ca eva varṣāṇām kathayāmi samāsatas anyeṣām ca eva dvīpānām vividha vihita āgatiḥ bhāratasya varṣasi anava bhedāḥ prakīrtitāḥ indradvīpaḥ kaśeruśva tāmraparṇaḥ gabhastimant nāgaddīpaḥ tathā asaumyaḥ gāndharva śrvāraṇaḥ tathā ayam tu navabhaḥ teṣām dvīpaḥ sāgara saṃgataḥ svādūdakaḥ nāma nāmnā sāgara uttaratas mahān tasya ca adya aparā pṛthvī dviguṇena pramāṇāt tasmāt param ca vailokaḥ lokālokaḥ ca nāmnaḥ lokān viśati tat lokṛ pramāṇam loka vistarāt manasā asiddhi saṃpanna anīroga aśvira jīvinaḥ prākāra sthitayaḥ ca eva sauvarṇa aśva saha arṇavāḥ lokeśāḥ ca eva catvāraḥ lokālokesthitāḥ tathā evam sa bhuvi vistāraḥ triguṇaḥ parimāṇāt iti śrī śiva mahā purāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām saptadvīpavarṇanaṃ nāma tṛtīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ tu mayā ākhyātaḥ vistāraḥ dīrgha tā tathā adhastāt yat pravakṣyāmi tāla tala vāsinām tatra bhogavatī ramya nānā ratna upaśobhitā sarve ca nāga rājānām viśramante mudā anvitāḥ tatra siddhā muni gaṇāḥ bharata ādyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ bāliyaḥ pavanaḥ nāma nāgaḥ pūraṇaḥ eva ca maṇimālaḥ ca eva bhadronāgaḥ ca eva atha kauśikaḥ bala aśvatarau ubhau karavīra puṇḍarī kausaṃvataḥ atha mahoragaḥ te ca anyena agapata anantāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ purī bhogavatī ramyā nānā ratna upaśobhitā vicitrābhiḥ patākābhiḥ vimānaiḥ vimānaiḥ sahasraśas dolā laṃbita vāsā aśva muktā dāmaiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ hāsya nāṭya vicitrābhiḥ gāna vāditra niḥkhanaiḥ sarva kāma prasiddha arthāḥ śva apsarasā upamāḥ na eva teṣām bhavet glāniḥ na śokaḥ na jarā tathā bhayam na asti sarva kāma hite ratāḥ puṣṭidānasyara hitāḥ sarva kāmeṣu pūjitāḥ tatra bhogavatī ramyā prabhā lokā dvi śiṣyate tatra stambha sauvarṇāni sauvarṇāni samaṃtataḥ vajra vaiḍūrya kalpāni mahāratnāni śobhitā indranīla mahānīlaiḥ sarvataśva abhimaṇḍitā sarva kālaphala anayaḥ sarva pāyasa kardamāḥ anna parvata kūṭāḥ ca śaṅkha kunda indu pāṇḍurāḥ kalpitāḥ a brahmanā pūrṇāḥ śaṃkarasya ājñayā purā payasā anitya pūrṇāni bhājanāni samaṃtataḥ madhukulyāḥ ca saṃnyastāḥ ārakta dantāḥ ati śobhitāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ tathā ca anyā bhāryā yauvana saṃpadaḥ bhukta abhuktāḥ priyaiḥ tatra yoniḥ tāsām na cakṣatā prasūtāyāḥ tu kanyāyāḥ yau vanam na apihīyate ti sva dāra niratāḥ sadā iṣṭa bhuj sva jana ākīrṇa a nāga loke prakīrtitāḥ madhya tiryañc gatiḥ khyātā a tāsām taṣām anekaśas nāga lokasya vistāram dviguṇam parikīrtitam eka deśa pramāṇena mayā ākhyātam yathā tathā yojanaiḥ koṭire kātunāga lokaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ūrdhva tiryañc prasaṃkhyātam catur asram tathā dvijāḥ taram pravakṣyāmi hiraṇyapura vāsinām tatra api koṭiḥ saṃkhyātā ayojanaiḥ parimāṇāt tatra āsan sa phala vaṅkṣāḥ puṣpaiḥ ca eva sugandhinaḥ nānā vicitra nirghoṣa niḥsvanaiḥ pūrṇa kandaraiḥ yauvana sthāḥ striyaḥ tatra sukumārāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ puruṣa a rūpa saṃpannāḥ sva dāra nirata iṃdriyāḥ sauvarṇa aśva gṛhāḥ tatra vimāna cāriṇaḥ sarve sarve ca sthita yauvanāḥ akṣata pratimāḥ tatra striyaṃśu apsarasā upamāḥ hukla danta ambara dharāḥ candra aṃśu vimala prabhāḥ manoramāḥ su siddhārthāḥ cakravāka sadharmiṇaḥ na udvegaḥ ūna ca kopaḥ tu īrṣyā asūyā vivarjitāḥ saṃtye te prahāda ādyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ teṣām prasādāt jīvanti sarva lokān na saṃśayaḥ brahma ādyāḥ devatāḥ sarvā ādhāryate samanantaram para aparāṇām lokānām dhāraṇaiḥ loka dhāraṇaiḥ sarvān imān dhārayati surabhiḥ nāma nāmnaḥ pṛthvīm dhārayati sarvān sudhanvā nāma nāmnaḥ sulabhāca uttarām diśam dakṣiṇām caṣakānām adhārayanti diśam sadā teṣām prasādāt jī vanti brahma ādyāḥ tridivaukasaḥ tasmin adivyāni veśmāni citrāṇi ca laghūni ca patākā dhvaja citrāṇi prāsādānām ca paṅktayaḥ sarva kāmaphalā vṛkṣa aramya aśvitra aśvitra aśca pādapāḥ svargāt atitarām ramyā sukhasparśā jalāśayāḥ yāmyānām a purā utyeṣā asadā a sampūrṇa mānasā brahmanā a vihita apūrvaiḥ kāma rūpa guṇa anvitā mājanā ni sahasraśas sarvaiḥ ca eva sukha sparśāḥ śvāraṇasya api veśmani śubhāḥ prakīrtitāḥ pāyasena ca pūrṇāni bhājanāni saha sraśas saṃnyastāni ca dṛśyate ambu divya amṛta upamam bhaktāḥ nānāvidhāḥ tatra bhūṣaṇāḥ pūrṇaiḥ kalpitāḥ mā na śakyāḥ nāma mātreṇa ākhyātum su samāhitaiḥ uddeśa mātram kathitāḥ pātāle asmin guṇa āmayā teṣām vakṣyāmi vaivipra anāgapātāla vāsinām citra avicitrāḥ kurvāṇāḥ sūkṣmāṇi ca gṛhāni ca dṛśyante tāni nityam hi avyakta avyakta saṃjñitāḥ tad anaṃtasya pātāle parikīrtitā guṇāḥ saṃkhyāna rahitāḥ tasmin puravare tadā tattvāt tasya api anantasya sarva kāma su pūjitā atas param tu vipra indra śṛṇuṣva ekamanāḥ kathām vaitariṇīyāt asipattravanam ca eva yamaśūlī bhaya āvahā bhairavāṇi ca rūpāṇi eka pāṣāṇam eva ca malam śālmalī karṣaṇam adhamaḥ strīghātī pūti māṃsa icaniḥ kṣiptaḥ kṣiptaḥ dhana dhānya suvarṇāni hiraṇyam vā aviśeṣatas hṛtvā narakam āpnoti yama śūlam bhaya āvaham mātṛ naḥ sūci mukhena śatam varṣāṇi pīḍanam pitṛ hantā urvaṃtu sura uttamāḥ ūcuḥ sraṣṭā tvam paripṛ cchasi varāṇām vai sahasrāt tu darśanam deva śasyate mahān naḥ saṃśayaḥ atyantam bhagavān vaktum arhati durlabham paramam gutyam praṣṭavyam praśnam uttamam avartamāna āśvaye bhaktāḥ parameśvare tevaśyavāsinām tulya munīnām bhāvitātmanām bhava pāpam na vidanti teḥ yāti paramām gatim na deva asura gandharva an ayakṣān a carākṣasāḥ saha rudra bhaktāḥ tu vipra indrāḥ prāpnuvanti śiva ālayam aśubhāḥ pāpa karmāṇaḥ yena raiḥ kalmaṣīkṛtāḥ īśvaram pratipaśyam dvija abhāvita bhāvanāḥ mahādevam prabhum prabhavatām api ye smaraṃti sadā rudra bhayam teṣām na vidyate suraiḥ sahavāsam iti śeṣaḥ śivālayam śivakalyāṇam ca tad ālaya sthānam mokṣam iti arthaḥ prabhavatām alaukika śaktimatām devānām pāpa yonayaḥ śvapaca ādayaḥ nīlakaṇṭhasya nīlaḥ kaṇṭhaḥ viṣa bhakṣaṇena yaṃsyasaḥ sarva lakṣaṇa hīnaḥ sarvaiḥ nija varṇa āśrama ucita dharma ihi naḥ tam devadevam maheśvaram rudra rudra iti tri saṃdhyam yaśva būyāt vicakṣaṇaḥ bhāga kīrtanāt nīlakaṇṭhasya sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate sarva lakṣaṇa hīnaḥ api yuktaḥ vā sarva pātakaiḥ marvaṃtarati tad pāpam bhāvāt śivam āsthitaḥ pāpa yoniṣu yat bhavet mahādeva prapannānām bhayam teṣām na vidyate manasā api śirva devam ye prapayanti mānavāḥ vidhūtāḥ sarva pāpebhyaḥ devaiḥ saha ramanti te agnihotram cayet nityam yajñān ca eva su dakṣiṇān rudra bhaktasya vipra indrāḥ kalām nāḥ īti ṣoḍaśīm sarveṣām dhyāna yogānām ye ca anye mokṣa kāṅkṣiṇaḥ mahādeva prasādena prāpnuvanti parām gatim a prāpya cavi rūpa akṣaṃkaḥ pumān siddhim arhati tīrthānām ca mahā tīrtham maṃgalā nāṃca maṃgalam īśvaram sarva bhūta patiḥ bhavaḥ hṛdisthaḥ sarva bhūtāḥ nāma oṃkāram adhigacchati mahā liṅga lakṣaṇam aśāmyaśamana karam katham tad phalam vidmahe yathā ghṛtam ca payasi yayā agniḥ ca eva dāruṇi yathā avayam tathā ca anye tathā asana tkumāra ādayaḥ mādhyātmikaiḥ sura varaiḥ brahmanaḥ sva ātma sambhavaiḥ tad kāraṇakā aiti bhāvaḥ om namaḥ prakṛtya jāpyam stuti homa liṅgam nataḥ bravīmi atra mahā maheśvaram punar tu tatra api dadarśa liṃgam anāmaya liṃgam alakṣaṇam ca tad yakṣa adhipa pannaga adhipāḥ vibhum prapaśyanti maheśvaram param mahā viṣam yojarayat kṣaṇena mānuṣa nāgānām na bhayam vidyate kvacid mānavāḥ arcayanti virūpākṣa liṅga mūrti maheśvaram iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭi varṣa śatāni ca hṛṣīkeśeṇa vipra indraiḥ varṣa koṭim prasāditaḥ mahādevaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ maheśvaraḥ tuṣṭena ca tathā viṣṇuḥ varaiḥ śveṣṭhaiḥ tu yojitaḥ mahā cakradhara uvalī īśvarasya prasādena viṣṇuḥ parama taijasaḥ rakṣate pṛthivīm sarvām ajeya śva balī tataḥ prasāditaḥ virūpākṣaḥ puṣkarākṣaḥ maheśvaraḥ iṣṭābhiḥ stuti pūjābhiḥ vividhaiḥ karmabhiḥ tathā mahādevaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ hiraṇmayaḥ tuṣṭena ca kṛtaḥ brahmā saṃhartā viśvatomukhaḥ dātā āhartā aca goptā ca saṃhartā ca yugeyuge pitāmaha tvam ca sura asurāṇām brahma ādhipatyam param avyayam ca anāgatam vartamānam śvam sarveṣu sarve ca vedāḥ saha ṣatiḥ aṅgaiḥ sāṃkhyam ca yogam ca sa pāribhāṣam mahat vāyubhakṣaḥ abukṣavat durvāsas śvarma saṃvṛtaḥ evam āsīt virūpākṣaḥ rudraḥ tuṣṭaḥ vai kṛttivāsāḥ pinākadhṛk bhūyas cakratu rājena dattam ca eva triviṣṭapam sanatkumāraḥ putraḥ ume vyākhyātaḥ mānasa uddijāḥ sahasram ca vimānānām sapta saṃkhyāsu yat purā candra sūrya prakāśeṣu vibhāneṣu pratiṣṭhitaḥ strī sahasra samākīrṇaḥ dīpyamānaḥ su tejasā gāyadbhiḥ nṛtyamānaiḥ a vādayadbhiḥ a sarvaśas puruṣaiḥ sūrya saṃkāśaiḥ dīpyamānaiḥ sva tejasā upaviṣṭaḥ sthitaḥ tatragi riṃ pādena pīḍayan yajamāna āśvaye dṛṣṭa āloka yātrā kara āśvaye te tam āsādya sarva dhiṣṇyeṣu adhiṣṭhitāḥ udyoginām ca tarji tvam bhīruṇām ca nivāraṇam puṣpa kāle ca puṣyanti phala kāle phala pradāḥ pāka kāle saṃvṛtāḥ māśritāḥ ye ca nakṣatra mārgeṣu nakṣatrāṇi samāśritāḥ caṃdra sūrya augra saṃtiye sva sthāne prasthita aśvāḥ anye sāṃkhya yogam anuvratāḥ asaṃkhyāta atyaneka aśva jaṅgama ajaṃgamāḥ sthitāḥ samāśritāḥ divyāḥ pārśva gatāḥ sarve gṛhāḥ tu pādapāḥ tathā kunda indu kumuda prakhyām māla padma sugandhinīm teṣām varṇa viśeṣaḥ asti pramāṇam ca eva dṛśyate ekaikasya gaṇeśasya śarīram pratitiṣṭhati meru mandara śailānām gaṇānām parimāṇāt teṣām parivṛtaḥ udevaḥ grahānām iva bhāskaraḥ sanatkumāraḥ deveśaḥ gaṇeśāya mahātmane evam dṛṣṭam mayā ākhyātam bhīmasya amita tejasaḥ śṛṇuyāt gaṇa saṃkhyānam manasā api sadā smaret prayatna mānasaḥ bhūtvā paṭhet parvaṇi parvaṇi sarvān kāmān avāpnoti amṛta tvam ca viṃdati śatam śata sahasrāṇi rudra loke mahīyate tathā eva samudāharet hāra kāle tu paṭhet rāhmaṇānām ca saṃnidhau nityam evam paṭhati yaḥ śraddhāna ujita indriyaḥ śata rudra phalam tasya labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ paṭhataḥ tu tatas puṇyam gaṇa saṃkhyām ca nityaśas śṛṇuyāt vā piyaḥ bhaktyā sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate prabhāta samaye kāle samutthāya mahā manāḥ brahmānam deva kartāram sarva śāstra viśāradam siddhāḥ te garvitāḥ purā vā ukta gaṇa varṇa nasya pāṭha śravaṇa ādiṣu phala viśeṣam āham ityādi śata śata sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām iti śeṣaḥ mogha retas sa phala śukra ananta pāpa yuktaḥ vā ūrdhva canayanam dṛṣṭvā deva tejas mayam sthitam pitāca pitara ume dyat dṛṣṭvā apātram upāgatāḥ evam dṛṣṭvā āsa mām putraḥ vyājahāra sa sambhramaḥ nigṛhītaḥ asmi bhadram te bālena akṛtakarmaṇā mānāni ca ratnāni ajasram ca susaṃskṛtam tena aham duḥkha saṃtāpāt deham tyakṣye na saṃśayaḥ ātmānam gamayāmāsa dhyāna yogena dṛṣṭavan jñātvā tatas dṛṣṭa naraḥ bhavat utthāya ca āsa na a brahmā a prāñjaliḥ praṇataḥ sthitaḥ namaskṛtvā mahādevam īśvaram sarvatomukham idam āha mahā tejā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ yogānām adhikaḥ yogī devānām ambikāpatiḥ dṛṣṭvā purā nandi mukha deva devena bhāṣitam anugraham mahādevaḥ kartu kāmaḥ maheśvaraḥ ha ātmā ca eva su durlabhaḥ tu ete viṣṇunā ca prakīrtitāḥ na kiṃcid rahmacārī ca paśyati akṛtabuddhyaḥ ca aikāntena ca saukhya iva anāsti tatra vicāraṇā vṛṇīṣva ātmam mahādevam gāṇapatyam su durlabham ca brahmanaḥ vacanam śrutvā aprayata amāna saṃjapan mahādevaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ maheśvaraḥ tuṣṭaḥ prasannaḥ deveśaḥ karmabhiḥ śva amita ojasaḥ sthitaḥ pradakṣiṇaḥ rutvā devadevasya dhīmataḥ prīti cārī dharmiṣṭhaḥ vara daḥ varaḥ dhāraṇam sarva bhūtānām dharādhara patiḥ yamaḥ mahā bhūta saṃsāra daśa īśvaraḥ sāṃkhya yoga īśvaraḥ karma kumāraḥ kamala īkṣaṇaḥ mahā sūrya agni netra śva cāru netra vibhūṣitaḥ catur mukhaḥ catur daṃṣṭraḥ catuḥ bahuḥ catur yugaḥ vāhanaḥ mahādhāraḥ hari kārttikaḥ śrīkaṇṭhaḥ kali nāśanaḥ deva adeva asura parāyaṇaḥ kapardī śūla hastaḥ ca ajātaḥ parama āgatiḥ tāpasānām param tattvam tathā ca paramam padam parāvara jñaḥ lokānām sarvadā harivāhanaḥ asitāṅgaḥ sitāṅgaḥ ca asitāyatalocanaḥ brahmaṇā adhīyate brahmā asaṃsthitaḥ nābhi paṅkaje madhu yajūṃṣi sāmāni kalpa upaniṣadaḥ tathā mantrāṇām bhavanam ca eva parasya ātharvaṇasya ca sahasravāh paśupatiḥ sahasra śata yojanaḥ bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyam ca bhagavant eva sarvaśas tvad gātrebhyaḥ yaḥ lokāḥ saḥ nātanāḥ evam saṃstūyamānaḥ saḥ vyaktī bhūtaḥ maheśvaraḥ upagamyam udāyuktaḥ tadā adṛṣṭaḥ sa dṛṣṭimān tad kamaṇḍalu dhara udaṃḍī śaśāṅka kṛta śekharaḥ vyāghra carma ambara dharaḥ siṃha camaṃcara chadaḥ nāga yajñopavītī ca akṣamālā vibhūṣitaḥ maṭī śikhaṇḍī khadvāṅgī paṭṭiśa aśani śūladhṛk tatas śara dharaḥ devaḥ śakti cāpa sa mudgaraiḥ śaṅkha cakra gadā pāṇiḥ padma śūka hala āyudhaḥ mālī ghora cāpa dhṛk mahā ārūḍha ūr̤hī īpyamānaḥ gaṇaiḥ parivataḥ haraḥ nandinā śūla hastena purastāt darśitaḥ prabhuḥ dadṛśe bhagavān devaḥ sūrya agni śaśinā dṛśā tathā ca sarva prāṇi rūpā eti bhāvaḥ brahmanā akathitam pūrvam yathāgatyam yathodbhavam manasaḥ kāma lobhau melobhāt meha ṛṣaṇam ca yat indriyāṇām ca sarveṣām indriyāṇi manāṃsi ca māneṣu udāna udāna me tat tat tat sarva bhūtānām niṣpattiḥ samudāhṛtā na aśnaṃti tarpitāḥ devāḥ sadā viśada mānasaḥ tvam eva uraga gandharva piśāca yakṣa rākṣasāḥ tvat ṛte na anya bhaktaḥ asmi manasā karmaṇā a girā tasya evam vacanam śrutvā umāpatiḥ maheśvaraḥ mama mad nāmāni sarvāṇi gocarāṇi bhavantu te su saṃgrahāni sarvāṇi na asti kācid vicāraṇā pārāśarya aiti khyātaḥ utpatsyati mahā tapāḥ saḥ sa dharma ātmā ajñānavān dīrghadarśanaḥ bhaviṣyati mala vimala śuddham jñānam candra sama prabham rathaṃkāma gamam divyam sāra ratna vibhūṣitam muktā jāla paricchanna hema jāla samāvṛtam tatra sevyamānam sura asuraiḥ mānam sūrya saṃkāśam sarva loka ujvalam śubham asuraiḥ akṣaram tatra aiśvaryam bhaviṣyati mama ājñayā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitā āryā aṣṭamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sa saṃcacāra lokān trīn brahma putraḥ abikāsutaḥ aiṣa ḍhātāca kartāca saṃha rtāca yugeyuge etasya trividham sarvam īśānasya mahātmanaḥ eṣa yajñapatiḥ devaḥ kṛtāṃtaḥ saumāpatiḥ eṣa hotā ācahomi aśvaḥ evam yajña vidaḥ viduḥ indriyāṇi indriya artheṣu sarvaḥ eva maheśvaraḥ evam jñāna param brahma praśāntam nirmalam śivam avyaktam ca avyaktam ca jñānam ca ajñānam eva ca sāṃkhya yogam param sāṃkhya yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati tatas jñānena śuddhāḥ tu prāṇāyāma jita iṃdriyāḥ dhyāyanti parama oṃkāram yoginām paramam padam tapasām ca prasādena labhaṃte yoga citakāḥ śrutiḥ iyam parama śivasya gutyam śrutvā paramaiḥ saḥ evam śrutvā tatas sarve ṛṣayaḥ dharma vatsalāḥ abhyanujñāpyatām deva gacchāmaḥ vigata eṣaṇāḥ yaiḥ dhūpaiḥ alaṃkāraiḥ stūyate vividhaiḥ śivaḥ oṃkāra ādi namaskāraiḥ sahitaiḥ gīta vādanaiḥ suvratāḥ na jñānena na tapaḥ sā ciṃtanāt bhāvitātmanām sāṃkhyāt eva param mokṣam yat ca anyaiḥ vividhaiḥ tathā ṛṣibhiḥ viprayuktān vaiṛṣīṇām pradadau rān teṣām api yathākāmam manasā īpsitam dadet sarva varṇa anukampī ca sarva tīrtha mayaḥ vyayaḥ yeṣām tu kalaṣa abuddhiḥ narāṇām bhāvitātmanām mūrti viśanti vidvasaḥ janāḥ tad khyātāḥ bhaviṣyanti śiva āśritāḥ yaḥ ca enām tyaṃ yaḥ ca enām śṭaṇuyāt sadā devāgāre paṭhet nityam sadā brāhmaṇa saṃnidhau tad dhyāya phala śrutiḥ asti viṣkambhena argala rūpeṇa āyāmataitiyāvat iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām bahmagītā nāma navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tat aham jñātum icchā mā vistareṇa mahā mune āsīt giri varaḥ vyāsa yojanānām samaṃtataḥ aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi nadī prasravaṇaiḥ yutaḥ viṣkambhena sthitaḥ brahman tāvān eva ucchritaḥ smṛtaḥ prabhaḥ tasya kumbhepu kumbheṣu kandareṣu darīṣu ca nānā kusuma citra ipu śikhinām madhurā giraḥ bheruṇḍaiḥ svarṇa yūthaiḥ va cakāraiḥ anviteṣu ca kīrṇeṣu ca eva bhavaneṣu ca harmya stambheṣu kīrṇe pusiṃhānām rūpa śālinām hobhita giri varye ca devānām ca surā gaṇāḥ kubera pramukhāḥ yakṣāḥ krīḍanti ca samantataḥ vicaranti mudā yuktāḥ vidyādhara gaṇa anvitāḥ tamburu pramukhāḥ tathā anvitāḥ yantra dhārā nighāteṣu ninadaṃti śikhaṇḍinaḥ tāḥ tucam drāṃśubhāḥ kāmaṃjyotsnāyāḥ sarit uttamāḥ tatra sā āpatate gaṃgā devatānām kulāni vai teṣu ca ātmani vā bhānti udita anni samam tatas tam prāpya sarva bhūtāni sauvarṇāni mahanti vai na ca api sama ṛṣayoḥ vāti vai mārutāḥ śubhāḥ manasā tat na paśyanti devatāḥ grāma ha ṛṣayaḥ bhuvanam kāñcana śrīman vijayam vijayā nadī yojanānām sahasrāṇi daśa ca aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ tāpanīyena mahatā prākāreṇa samāvṛtāḥ tatra su ramya aśva patākā śobhi māli kāḥ divākara kara ābhāḥ ca su prabhāḥ amita ojasaḥ tatra dvāra sahasrāṇi tāvam dvijottamāḥ sarva aṇi puṇya karmāṇi taru ṇa arka sama prabhāḥ vinyastaiḥ pūrṇa kumbhaiḥ ca śobhitāni yathā tathā muktā dāmaiḥ su vipulaiḥ bhūṣitāni samaṃtataḥ puṣpa upahāraiḥ vividhaiḥ dhūpaiḥ ca agaru sambhavaiḥ rakṣibhiḥ śva samāguptam vipula aiśvarya śālibhiḥ prākāra pratisaṃchanna prāsādaiḥ gṛha paṅktibhiḥ yailāsa śikhara prakhyā virājata sahasraśas anyāḥ jāmbūnada mayāḥ prāsādānām ca paṃktayaḥ pāvakāḥ iva dīpyate jvālā vipula mālinaḥ kecid maṇi mayāḥ tatra prāsāda ābhavana uttamāḥ prerayan nidiśaḥ sarvāḥ śaradi iva uditāḥ grahāḥ bhūmikābhiḥ paricchinnam kānanaiḥ ca samaṃtataḥ gavākṣa mālā kalitam muktā dāmaiḥ vibhūṣitam vicitraiḥ bhūṣitaiḥ naddham dvāraiḥ su vipulaiḥ śvitraiḥ śobhita aṃsa paricchadaiḥ nānā ratna śataiḥ śvitraiḥ patākā śata śobhitaiḥ vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpaiḥ phala ādyaiḥ ca phalānām ca suvarṇitaiḥ pārijātaka varṇaiḥ aiśva sauvarṇa kadala vanaiḥ nadībhiḥ śva taḍāgaiḥ śva palvalaiḥ śva samantataḥ yāpībhiḥ dīrghikābhiḥ śvanhadaiḥ kūpaiḥ ca śobhitaiḥ balākānām capam ktibhiḥ mayūraiḥ cakravākaiḥ śva tathā eva śuka sārikaiḥ tasmin advāra purāṇi aṣṭa pura śreṣṭhe dvijottamaiḥ hi śrīdvāram prathamam tatra mahā asi yaḥ vyavasthitaḥ pūrvasyām diśi vaiśaivaḥ padma mālā vibhūṣitaḥ kṣmīdvāram tatas tasya yatra ambuda sama prabhaḥ mahākālaḥ mahā kāyaḥ sthitaḥ śūlaḥ mahā balaḥ śivam nāma puram tatra dakṣiṇena vyavasthitam saṃnidhāne tathā ca anya etasyām eva diśi dijāḥ pālitam bhīma nādena gaṇeśena mahātmanā paścimam vāruṇam dvāram tatra nandīśvaraḥ śrutaḥ mat jivhena gaṇanāthena dhīmatā kīrtidvāram tathā udīcyām tasyām eva diśi dvijāḥ yatra arka varuṇa prakhyaḥ dvāra adhyakṣaḥ maheśvaraḥ upakrīḍanakaiḥ śvitraiḥ krīḍate bhagavant prabhuḥ yatra yānti jita krodha ajita lobha ajita indriyāḥ śrūyaṃte paśupateḥ bhaktyā rudra bhakti pare dvijāḥ ye ca eva āgama saṃyuktāḥ sāṃkhyāḥ ca śrutabuddhayaḥ nyāyāt yudhyamānāḥ na aśva saṃgrāma abhimukha īhatāḥ kṣatriya ugograhasya arthe mitra artha irāṣṭra pālane mad mad mad as as ye suvarṇasya dātāraḥ tathā sarva priyaṃvadāḥ veda adhyayana saṃpannāḥ dhyāyinaḥ vrata cāriṇaḥ yajati vidhinā ayajñaiḥ kratubhiḥ śvāru dakṣiṇaiḥ te tatra gatvā adṛṣṭāḥ tu nivasaṃti yathāsukham kalpa ayuta sahasrāṇām sahasrāṇi caturdaśa parame jagatīm ca abhinaṃdaṃti ciram pramuditāḥ tathā tatas param pravakṣyāmi raupya bhṛṅga nivāsitam rājataṃgiri rājasya śṛṅgam śrīsāgaram mahat yojanānām sahasrāṇi trīṇi evam tu param hitam prākāreṇa atha mahatā rāja tena samāvṛtam alaṃkṛtena divyena patākā dhvaja mālinā rājata dvāra sāhasaiḥ maṇi citraiḥ śva citritam tatra stambha sahasrābhyām dvābhyām prāsādam uttamam pura madhye tam rājatam dhātu bhūṣitam nānā viṣṇu padam nāma tat suraiḥ api kīrtitam catur dvāram catur śṛṅga kailāsa śikhara prabham nānā ratna samākīrṇa nānā druma latā āvṛtam tasya mūrdhani sthite dvāre kṛṣṇa rūpaḥ pratāpavān dvārādhyakṣaḥ sthitaḥ tatra hṛd yajña karaḥ balī pratīhāraḥ mahākāyaḥ hariprāṇa samaḥ jave tasmin madhumatī nāma nadī sva artha prakāśakā pāñcanaiḥ kamalaiḥ śvāpi nānā pakṣi nināditā tatra atha su ciram kālaṃbhaya śoka vivarjitāḥ tebhiḥ tebhiḥ karmabhiḥ ādiṣṭāḥ śaktitas yaśasvinaḥ upalabhya smṛti devāḥ tatra eva śaraṇam gatāḥ brahmā viṣṇuḥ ca śakraḥ ca ūcuḥ tatra aumāpatim tvam kumāraḥ kumāraḥ tvam jātaḥ tvam sarvatomukhaḥ oṃkāraḥ tvam vai paṭkāraḥ daṇḍaiḥ nītiḥ prasādāt bhaviṣyatha svacchanda svarga loke maheśvarāḥ evam uktvā tu bhagavān tatra eva antaradhīyata punar sṛṣṭeṣu lokeṣu brahmā tatra prajāpatiḥ tribhiḥ māsaiḥ avāpnoti śiva liṅga arcane rataḥ samyak iṣṭa phalāḥ sarve śānta adāṃtāḥ samādheḥ nava māsān samārādhya brāhmaṇaḥ vijita indriyaḥ mavān mandaraḥ meruḥ kailāsaḥ gandhamādanaḥ vālakhilyāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ naimiṣeyāḥ ta podhanāḥ yāḥ ca eva apsarasaḥ divyāḥ yeca mātṛ gaṇāḥ tathā tārā gaṇāḥ graha gaṇāḥ sarve pitṛ gaṇāḥ tathā siddhāḥ tathā eva ca bhāṇam paramam jñātvā liṅgam yaḥ arcayate naraḥ tasmin bahu guṇām prīti karoti vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ ekān hi tat avāpnoti śiva liṅga arcaneḥ atas trīṇi aṣṭau yāni sthānāni yat phalam labhate naraḥ eka aham tat avāpnoti vipraḥ liṅga arcane rataḥ kumāraḥ brahmaṇaḥ putraḥ pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ nandīśvaraḥ gaṇaśreṣṭhaḥ mahākālaḥ ca vīryavān bhṛṅgu aṃgirā marīci śva dadhīci śva yamaḥ tathā tathā śukra bṛhaspatī dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ śreṣṭhaḥ dakṣa putrāḥ tu samavai atriḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ bhagavān kāśyapa śva mahā tapāḥ gautamaśva bharadvājaḥ viśvāmitraśva kovidaḥ maruta śva tathā aśvinaḥ sādhya a vidyādhara a nāgāḥ ṛṣayaḥ viśva devatāḥ tat kṣāra udaḥ puṣkaraḥ gaṅgā śmaśānāni ca sarvaśas yat krīḍate bhagavant bhūtaiḥ bālaḥ krīḍanakaiḥ iva vyākulīkṛtāḥ brahma ādyāḥ ṛṣayaḥ devāḥ tat mama nigadataḥ śṛṇuḥ raṇaḥ yamaḥ kālaśva mṛtyuśva varuṇaḥ dhanada unalaḥ upacāra viśeṣeṇa phala itāratamyam vadati daśa sāvarṇikam pañca kṛṣṇalakaḥ māṣaḥ eti mānam anusṛtya ṣaṣṭi adhika śata māṣa suvarṇa nirmitam tapas bhaktyā valmīka mṛttikāsu ca puṣpa upahāraiḥ dhūpaiḥ atulyam phalam avāpnuyāt daśa aparādhān toyena kṣīreṇa eva śatam kṣamet prīra srānam ghṛta abhyaṅgaḥ sa ghṛtam guggulam tathā daśa sauvaṇikam puṣpam yaḥ bhavāya prayacchati yam yam kāmayate kāmam tam tam pūrayate śivaḥ mālayā śatasāhakhyā jāpyam daśaguṇam smṛtam vidhiyajñāt japa yajñaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ daśabhiḥ guṇaiḥ upāṃśu syāt śataguṇaḥ sahasromānasaḥ smṛtaḥ tṛṇāni auṣadhi gulmāni latā vallīḥ tathā eva ca tathā eva sarva vṛkṣāṇām puṣpam pattram phalam tvacam puṣpāṇi bījāni śatadhā tathā mahādeva upayuktāni svarga yānti na saṃśayaḥ śraddadhānaḥ tu yaḥ kuryāt śuciḥ prayata mānasaḥ prāpya duḥkham na te sarve svarga yānti dvijottamāḥ mad aśva kārye pūrvam yathā naraiḥ liṅgam ca sthāpayet tatra vidhi pūrvam samāhitaḥ saṃvatsaram tu śuśrūṣām kṛtvā tatra śuciḥ naraḥ pūjā śva kārayet nityam tasya bhaktyā śivena vai pūjā artha pratyaham yaḥ tu gandha mālya āsa tam śubham saṃpādayet māhāt pāpa kṛt na sa dhārmikaḥ saṃpādayet atas pūjām pradṛṣṭena antarā ātmanā cira paryuṣitam mālyam bhavasya apanayet cayaḥ go sahasra phalam puṇyam prāpnuyāt na atra saṃśayaḥ tad pūrvasya ca liṅgasya śuciḥ prayata mānasaḥ yaḥ śūdra aśva mleccha aśva ye ca anye pāpa yonayaḥ jitaḥ dhīmatā puṇyābhiḥ adbhiḥ snānam ca candanena anulepanam tatas ca nivedanaiḥ sauvarṇaiḥ rājataiḥ kumbhaiḥ mṛd maya audumbare tathā mayaiḥ śuddhaiḥ sa bhṛṅgāraiḥ hiraṇmayaiḥ indranīlaiḥ mahānīlaiḥ tathā satatam ca arcayet devam śuciḥ prayata mānasaḥ tri kālam arcayet de vam śuciḥ prayata mānasaḥ mūrta yopi śivasya etāḥ tat mama nigadataḥ śṛṇu aiṃdrī īdra samāsthitā dvitīyā dakṣiṇā mūrtiḥ yā samāvṛtya tiṣṭhati tṛtīyā vāruṇī mūrtiḥ paśu imā tuṣṭi dām ama caturthī syāt tu varadā dhanadāsu sukha āvahā adhastāt pañcamī mūrtiḥ cacāra vidhinā atapaḥ ṣaṣṭhī vaiṣṇavī gatiḥ iṣyate ūrdhva ca mūrtiḥ āgneyī sarva bhūta pramardinī sarva bhūta sukha āvahā yatibhiḥ sevyate vyāsa jarā maraṇa bhīrubhiḥ anena vidhinā vyāsa yaśva jānāti īśvaram tena pāśupatam cīrṇa vimalam vratam avyayam mucyate evam vijñāya medhāvī bhaikṣa vṛtti samācaret mūrtīnām pravibhāgaḥ ca śiva liṅga arcanam tathā vividhāḥ sarvāsām api mūrtīnām pūjā arha dakṣiṇā aparā sā ca sṛjati bhūtāni tathā saṃharate prajāḥ vṛtti śraddhām sukham kāmam medhām ca eva prayacchati vividhān vidate kāmān mūrtiḥ sā dakṣiṇa aparā yadā sadā āyuktaḥ dakṣiṇāmūrtim arcayet mad yati sarvasvam niṣkalam ca yaṃdadet etat te kathitam vyāsa śiva liṅga arcanam param śraddhā kāma samāyuktāḥ te yānti paraḥ mām gatim darśanāt śravaṇāt dāpi nāma saṃkīrtanāt api pramāṇam ca eva liṅgasya śrutvā pāpaiḥ pramucyate striyaḥ striyaḥ icchā śvaye ca anye pāpa yonayaḥ ayasaṃśayaḥ śraddhā kāma samāyuktāḥ teyāṃti paramām gatim mahā nāma itihāsaḥ yaḥ brahmanā samudāhṛtaḥ krodha moha praśamanaḥ mahāpātaka nāśanaḥ yaḥ ca enam paṭhate nityam yaḥ ca enam śṭaṇuyāt naraḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām nāma kīrtanam nāma catudarśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca sthānāni yāni loke asmin yeṣu sannihitaḥ sadā sarveṣām teṣu yacchati anugraham satāṃtu bhajane samyak tuṣyate iva akathaṃtatas śṛṇu vyāsa parām vāṇīm sarva loka hitām śubhām bha gavān sāṃnidhyam kurute sadā nānā rūpa dharaḥ devaḥ sarva bhūteṣu vartata brahmā divākaraḥ viṣṇuḥ skandaḥ ca agniḥ puraṃdaraḥ arkaḥ somaḥ kuberaśva varuṇaśva api umāpatiḥ yaḥ hi yām devatām bhaktyā ārādhayati sarvatas tasya tām mūrtim āsthāya mahāde vaḥ prasīdati sthānānām parisaṃkhyānam vaktum śaktaḥ na ca kvacid api varṣa sahasraiḥ vāsa māsena tu mama śṛṇu me ca eva sarveṣām teṣu yaḥ vā api anugrahaḥ māheśvarīm imām sṛṣṭi śuciḥ bhūtvā niśāmaya mnā āmnā rudra padam śreṣṭha tathā māheśvaram padam śleṣmātakam tathā aproktam avimuktam mahālayam gokarṇa bhadrakarṇa icasvarṇa ākhyam sthānam aṣṭamam sthāneṣu eteṣu satatam sāṃnidhyam kurute bhavaḥ māheśvare tu bhagavant nityam pūjyaḥ tu śaṃkaraḥ dvi yojanam tu taiḥ kṣetram dakṣiṇa uttaratas smṛtam vistareṇa tu tāvat hi evam māheśvaram padam samāham āsthāya śivaḥ eva karoti iti āha yad eti māheśvaraṃcolī maheśvara eti nāmnā āloke prasiddham vārāṇasī mahālayamoṃkā praviśanti mṭatāḥ tatra parām māheśvarām tanum taiḥ ca eva piśācaiḥ pannagaiḥ tathā caturdaśam yojanam ca tat tu śleṣmātakam smṛtam deva dānava gandharva ṛṣayaḥ vatapodhanāḥ deva dānava gandharva ṛṣayaḥ vatapodhanāḥ mūjya saṃpūjya satatam śreṣṭhāḥ sadā rudra padebhavam ca ardha yojana vistīrṇa suvarṇa ākhyam viduḥ budhāḥ vārāṇasyām tu oṃkāra gamyaḥ viśveśvaraḥ sadā yate bhagavant devaḥ paramātmā asanātanaḥ viśveśvaram tu oṃkāram pra ṇamaṃti stuvaṃti ca tatra avimukte ca oṃkāraḥ nityam saṃnihitaḥ haraḥ devāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ ca eva tathā rājarṣayaḥ sadā mad naḥ nitya yoga āśva praśānta avīta kalmaṣāḥ upāsatesadā vyāsa pañcāyatana vāsinam aciṃtyānām atatrasthā tanuḥ devasya nirvṛtiḥ viśanti ca mahātmānaḥ parām māheśvarām tanum brahmā ca agni śva soma śva viṣṇuḥ indraḥ bṛhaspatiḥ upāsate mahābhāgam bhadrakarṇe sadāśivam tatra aham niyataḥ vyāsa gaṅgādvāre bhava priye etat mahādhanam nāma purāṇam puṇyam uttamam teṣu sthāneṣu vai pūrvam ṛṣayaḥ siddhim āgatāḥ divyā amāheśvara ābhogāḥ śaktiḥ yatra akṣayā aparā sthāna māhātmyam atulam puṇya pāpa praṇāśanam na anya bhaktāya dātavyam piśunāya śaṭhāya ca ślāghine ślāghamānāyai mama dharmya prakāśayet iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca sarvāṇi yāni tīrthāni guptāni āyatanāni ca teṣām puṇyam ca eva na hi mad tṛptiḥ asti iha śṛṇvataḥ vākyam uttamam māhātmya deva devasya śaṃkarasya mahātmanaḥ thṛṣyāmi satatam brahman param kautūhalam hime sanatkumāraḥ provāca vācā madhurayā tadā śṛṇu vyāsa parām vāṇīm vicitrām pāpa nāśinīm maṃgalān ca pavitrāṃca paṭhet parvasu parvasu idam sthāna māhātmyam iti pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ om namaḥ śivāya sthāna aṣṭakasya māhātmyam ukta sthānānām yātrāyāḥ vidhim āha rājasūya aśvamedhāni tad janyāni phalāni iti arthaḥ āha indra lokam sa gacchet tu dhārayan tu sadā aśuciḥ yāni uktāni pavitrāṇi svayam devena dhīmatā tāni te kathayiṣyāmi tasmāt ekam nāḥ śṛṇu chāga lāṅgam kuru ḍevā mukuṭa maṇḍala īśvaram ca eva gadagaṇḍa sthaleśvaram bhūta saṃghaiḥ taḥ prabhuḥ udivaukasaiḥ caturdaśa yojanānām sarveṣām hi parigrahaḥ ṛṣi gandharva juṣṭāni siddha rva ācaritāni ca thānāni etāni gutyāni rudreṇa sa gaṇenave vyuṣitāni sadā vyāsa devadevena śambhunā tarpayet tatra śṭaṇutasya api yat phalam rājasūya aśvamedhāni prāpnuvaṃti na saṃśayaḥ yaḥ vai pātayate prāṇān aśṭaṇu tasya piyā gatiḥ viśaṃti tu mahādevam tyakta jīvitāḥ muni gaṇa parivṛtam mahā tridaśa gaṇaiḥ abhiṣṭutam priyam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām śreṣṭha ākhyānam nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ phala bhogāḥ sa kāmānām ca huśaśva mahā yaśāḥ gutyānām api gutyā niśṭaṇu vyāsa samāhitaḥ yathā ca bhagavant devaḥ rutavan ca api anugraham purā vaiṛṣayaḥ vyāsampapracchuḥ dagdha kilbiṣāḥ muni tathā bhāgavatāḥ abhavan bhaktyā tutoṣabha gavān bhaktānām bhakta vatsalaḥ śravaṇa phalam āha iti viṣamam idam chandaḥ iti ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha saptadaśa ivyā kṛtavan anugraham teṣām darśanena maheśvaraḥ te praṇamya mahātmānaḥ bhūtānām īśvaram prabhum ūcuḥ prāñjalayaḥ bhūtvā vālakhilyāḥ tapodhanāḥ manasā a prārthitam yat ca tat kartā asau na saṃśayaḥ tatas te prīta manasaḥ dṛṣṭvā devam vṛṣadhvajam eṣa deva paraḥ pāraḥ yaha ṣṭaḥ bhagavant svayam icchāmaḥ bhagavan jñātum gukhyāni āyatanāni ca evam prasāditaḥ taiḥ tu munibhiḥ puṇya kāṃkṣibhiḥ uvāca tān ṛṣīn sarvān vākyena jīvayan iva śrī mahārudrā uvāca mama gutyam yeṣu nityam vasāmi aham trijām iti anugṛhṇāmi bhaktyā aparamayā asadā tān ivaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi apraśāntāya dātavyam na ca anya ahita kāriṇe yaḥ karkaśāya viśuddhāya piśunāya śaṭhāya ca capalāya nṛśaṃsa ayana deyam syāt kathaṃcana idam tu śreṣṭha putrāya śiṣyāya vahitāya ca idam tu śreṣṭha putrāya śiṣyāya vahitāya ca ślāghine ślāghamānāya praśāntāya tapasvine priyaṃvadāya śrotriyāya bhaktāya ca maheśituḥ tathā ājñā sma adbhutyam iti smṛtam gatvā tapasyataḥ nityam mānasam vi malam śivam tatra aham niyataḥ vipra gaṅgādvāre ca nityaśas sadāśivam gacchanti teṣām punarāvṛttiḥ bhavat mṛtyuḥ mahātmanām eṣa īśvara sadbhāvaḥ kathitaḥ te samāsatas yam sya upatiṣṭhati etat te kathitam puṇyam gutyānām ca eva kīrtanam tat su mahā puṇyam satyena eva mahā mune iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām māheśvaravarṇanaṃ nāma saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ iti saptadaśaḥ udhyāyaḥ uvāca suvrata prabhāvaiḥ karmaṇām ca eva kodhikaḥ vada īśvaraḥ etat mama saṃśayam tātaiḥ brūhi buddhimatām varaiḥ atra api udāharanti imam itihāsam purā tanam trailokya vijaya iviṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā baliḥ baddhaḥ mahā rāja trailokyam prāptavan tadā atha ājagmuḥ prabhum draṣṭum devadevam sanātanam yatra asau viśvarūpākṣaḥ kṣīrodasi asamīpatas siddhāḥ vidyādharāḥ nāgāḥ nadyaḥ sarva aśva parvatāḥ dṛṣṭavan bara tvam gatiḥ sarva devānām tvam yogī prabhuḥ avyayaḥ evam uktaḥ suraiḥ viṣṇuḥ siddha aiśva parama ṛṣibhiḥ pratyuvāca tatas viṣṇuḥ sarva gaḥ puruṣottamaḥ uvāca śrūyatām abhidhāsyāmi kāraṇam sura puṃgavāḥ yaḥ tuṣṭaḥ sarva bhūtānām khaṣṭṛ tvam adadāt śivaḥ sṛṣṭa aśva brahmaṇā ca eva sapta loka aśva māyayā tasya eva ca prabhāvena aham śreṣṭha tvam āgataḥ tad avastheṣu bhūteṣu ekaḥ ham śayitaḥ tathā sahasra śīrṣaḥ vai bhūtvā sahasra akṣaḥ sahasra pād māyayā avimala ambhasi etasmin antare dūrāt paśyāmi vimalam prabhum kṛṣṇa ajina dharam devam kamaṇḍalu vibhūṣitam iti iti kāraṇam sarvasya sukha duḥkhayoḥ mahā avidyā avidyā inalaḥ tathā indriyāṇām sarveṣām indriya arthāḥ smṛtāḥ sthaviṣṭhāḥ ca eva sūkṣmāḥ ca bhagavān eva sarvaśas hi viśva rūpaḥ mahā rūpaḥ sarva rūpaḥ tathā eva ca te te jasate iparam tejaḥ sparśāṇām sparśam eva ca rūpa gandha rasāḥ āpodhi paśca bhuvana īśvaraḥ ca vai chaṃdaḥ bhūtānām prabhuḥ avya yaḥ tvam kartā sarva bhūtānām lokeṣu pralaya aṃta kṛt tvam dhārayasi lokān trīn tvam eva sṛjasi prabho paścimena tuvatreṇa varuṇaḥ tvam prakāśase madityāḥ vasa vas rudrau aruṇa śva tathā aśvinaḥ siddha a vidyādhara a nāgāḥ apsaras yakṣa rākṣasāḥ siddhāḥ brahmarṣayaḥ ca eva cāraṇa aśva tapodhanāḥ vālakhilya aśva ṛṣayaḥ tapas siddhāḥ sahasraśas tvattaḥ prasūtā deveśaiḥ akṣarāśva mahā balāḥ sahasraśīrṣaḥ nantaḥ ca vai sukiḥ eva ca varuṇaśva mahātejā garuḍaśva mahā balaḥ arthaḥ dharma śva kāma śva yaśaḥ mohaḥ samīraṇaḥ agniḥ ca eva mahau viśva prajātāḥ te maheśvara ramā sītā tathā kālī devī gāyatrī eva ca antaram iti akṣara ajara amaraṇa śūnyāḥ lakṣmīḥ kīrtiḥ dhṛtiḥ siddhiḥ medhā lajjā vapuḥ smṛtiḥ tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ tathā ānandā ja yā devī sarasvatī tvattaḥ jātāḥ mahābhāga anye ca api mahā balāḥ ṛtuḥ saṃvatsaraḥ māsaḥ pakṣaḥ ahorātraḥ eva ca tathā nakṣatrāḥ nigrahāḥ ca eva aśvāgāvaḥ ajāvikāḥ rajobhiḥ māyayā āchannam na tvā paśyanti kevalam yoginaḥ nitya muktāḥ ye paśyanti tvām budhāḥ tathā māyayā a mohitam lokam tvad padam ca sanātanam na tvām paśyanti saṃmūḍhāḥ magnā tamasi dāruṇe mādau madhye tathā ca antena vidanti kadācana parātparaḥ parātparaḥ tvam paramam ca śāśvatam namaḥ stute bhasma vibhūti śīla namaḥ stute kāma śarīra nāśin namaḥ naga indra ātmaka devaiḥ nityam namaḥ astu te śaṃkaraiḥ nīlakaṇṭhaiḥ paṭṭiśam asi jātīyam kṣepaṇīyam śastram tat eva hetuḥ bhūtvā jagatkāraṇam bhūtvā sarva jit bhavati iti śeṣaḥ iti aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ evam saṃstūyamānaḥ hi kīrtyamānaḥ maheśvaraḥ babhāṣe ca tathā tuṣṭaḥ īśānaḥ vara daḥ prabhuḥ hi eka grīvaḥ su jaṭharaḥ nānā ābharaṇa bhūṣitaḥ nānā maṇi vicitra aṅgaḥ nānā gandha anulepanaḥ pināka dīpita karaḥ paṭṭiśa aśani śūladhṛk mahā yajña upavītī bhayaṃkaraḥ muktaḥ hāsaḥ tadā tena lokāḥ tatra prakampitāḥ tatas provāca bhagavant prītaḥ utha api āvayoḥ tathā ayam me dakṣiṇaḥ bā huḥ brahmā tvam hi mama ātmajaḥ mad bāhu śva me viṣṇu saṃyuge parājitaḥ munayaḥ sadṛśam samyak varam vṛṇuta suvratau tatas prahṛṣṭa manasau pādayoḥ patitau ubhau evam uktaḥ suraśreṣṭhaḥ sṛjadhvam vipulāḥ prajāḥ evam saṃkṣepāt proktaḥ prabhāvaḥ tasya yoginaḥ tena sarvam idam dṛṣṭa hetuḥ bhūtvā tu sarva jit idam ca svargyam āyuṣyam idam śāntikaram tathā tasya vighnam kurvati dānava agraha rākṣasāḥ bhuja gāḥ tathā yaḥ paṭhet aśuciḥ prātar brahmacārī jita iṃdriyaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām liṅgodbhavanāmā aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca abhyaṅge ca eva kim proktam kim phalam saptānām soma saṃsthānām yat phalam samudāhṛtam phalam vai sarva kāmyānām phalam bahu suvarṇakam ayuta arbuda koṭīnām teṣām aṣṭau yutāni ca tāḥ striyāḥ uvā puruṣaḥ uvā api yat iva atha napuṃsakaḥ māse māsetuyaḥ strāyāt yāvat jīvaṃrutī śuciḥ tathā eva ca catuḥ ṣaṣṭi sahasrāṇi gavām vā hema mālinām yaḥ dadyāt kapilānām tu kṣīra snānasya yat phalam māse māse triṣavaṇam yaḥ strāyāt muni puṃgavaḥ pakṣe pakṣe cayaḥ snāyāt yāvajjīvam dvijaḥ śuciḥ aparādha śatam devaḥ kṣamate na atra saṃśayaḥ puṣpa dānena tat puṇyam prāpnuyāt na atra saṃśayaḥ utpalam karavīram ca arka pallavakān tathā ājighrati campakam bilva pattram ca deve deyam sadā naraiḥ tat mama nigadataḥ śṛṇu apāmārga kuśān ca eva āśu ayukte nivedayet tathā asitāni puṣpāṇi yāvatkālam nivedayet caturṇām puṣpa jātīnām gandham āghrāti śaṃkaraḥ utpalānām sahasreṇa arka mama kaḥ viśiṣyate campakānām sahasreṇa dhattūram ca viśiṣyate dhattūraka sahasreṇa nāgapuṣpam viśiṣyate sindhu puppa sahasreṇa punnāga ntu viśiṣyate puṃnāgānām sahasreṇa karṇikāram viśiṣyate sindhupuṣpa sahasaiḥ tu bṛhatīnām viśiṣyate bilva pattrāt param na asti yena tuṣyati śaṃkaraḥ sarve śuddhāḥ su gandha āḍhya kṛṣṇanā eva nivedayet yatra ekam bilva pattrasya catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ udāhṛtam yathālābham yathāpakṣam puṣpāṇi nivedayet alābhena tu puṣpāṇām parṇāni tu nivedayet viśeṣeṇa tu yaḥ bhaktyā teṣām eka phalam śṛṇu mahā puṇyam rudra sāyujyam āvrajet iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām puṣpasāra samuddeśaḥ nāma ekonaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca bhūyas eva aham icchāmi īśvara ārādhanam katham jana prakāram abhidhāya jñāninām phala saṃsarga vimukhānām pūjā prakāram āha iti ekonaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ su lopa abhāve ārpaḥ śiva prītaye kāñcana dānasya phalam āha gaṇeśvara patiḥ nadī sūrya ayuta sama prabhaḥ māhātmyam pṛcchate nandikeśvaraḥ yathoktam pṛcchate devyā īśvareṇa mahātmanā uvāca mune maheśvareṇa pārvatyāḥ puratas bhi hitam purā yatra aham tatra saḥ nityam bhavet aṣṭaguṇa anvitaḥ tasya haimavate śṛṅge gṛham bāla arka saṃnibham yaḥ tu gāvaḥ hiraṇyam vāsam uddiśya pradāpayet tasya kāmadughām pṛthvīm dadāmi nirupadravām upahāra aiśva jāpya aiśva bhāvita aiśva api nityaśas agniṣṭoma agniṣṭoma ādibhiḥ yajñaiḥ yomā arcayati śobhane kasya ardhāsanam prāpya sura loke mahīyate sa yakṣāṇām guruḥ bhūtvā yakṣaḥ bhava ti vīryavān sthāpana abhyarcana mālyaiḥ dhūpa gandha anulepanaiḥ sureśvaram liṅge pūjām tu yā devī karoti mama śobhane abhyaṅgena pañcaśatam bhavet pañcaśatam devī trāpa na tu caturguṇam devi gīta vādya vara priye agarum śatasāhasam daśaguṇam candanam bhavet sarva mālyam pañcaśatam devi nirmālyam tat anantaram paṃcaguṇa kṛṣṇa aguruḥ smṛtaḥ aparādha sahasram ca kṣamate dubhāṣiṇi yat idam kṛṣṇasāram dahet tu mad muktau divyānām ca bhakta samānam tu devam sarva haram śivam ghṛta abhiṣekam yaḥ kuryāt saṃvatsaram ataṃdritaḥ mṛtyu vaśam gacchet gāṇapatyam tu bhokṣyate rudrāṇām sadṛśaḥ bhūtvā āraṣeṇa vicaret bhuvi tejaḥ maṇḍala saṃkāśam devam vrajati śakra vat caturdaśyām atha aṣṭamyām ubhau pakṣau vidhānāt bhakteḥ śivāya tasmāt jāti kāla ityādinā a niṣṭhā para nipātaḥ śiva dhyāne antarāyān āha bhāvanām dhyānam vinā api vidhinā ācitaḥ bhaktyā yathā bhāvitā eva phalam dāsyāmi anyathā abhāvakānām arcanam vinā na iti anvayaḥ arcāyām pratimāyām acitaḥ na tathā tuṣyati yathā acitaḥ tu tasya puṇya phalam devimat prasādāt idam śṛṇu śruti mātreṇa ye devi mama bhakti parāyaṇāḥ mad ad vai dadāmi kamala ānane yathāsthānāni sarvāṇi idam ya abhiracitāni ivai maheśvarī tathā ta iṣu mṛtyutaḥ na kadā bhayam yaḥ tu kāma kṛtam tyaktvā eka bhakti kṛtaḥ naraḥ tad vāc manas saṃyuktaḥ yāvat jīvan tu gacchati devitiṣṭhatitāvat ca yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam aneka vighna saṃbhūta atamasā bahulīkṛtāḥ tad ekāgra manasaḥ nityam paśyaṃti niścita āśvaye narāṇām alpa vittānām vidhinā abhāvanām vinā arcanam ca yathoktam vaigutyam vā api matam śṛṇu liṅga arcitaḥ yayātasya tuṣyāmi hariṇa īkṣaṇe arcitaḥ aham varārāhe pūjitaḥ sarva daivataiḥ dhūpaiḥ gedhaiḥ aśvamālyaiḥ ca rakta kāñcana vāsasaiḥ labhet bhaktyā aparamayā ayuktāḥ sakhyi yoga viśāradāḥ gacchanti mama lokān tu bhid naḥ mattaḥ su dāruṇaḥ tapasā atuna śaknoti draṣṭum mām devatāḥ api dhyānena eva niyuktā amām paśyaṃtidevinā anyathā sarva lokeṣu sarveṣām sāṃkhyā nārāyaṇā stutiḥ mad bhaktānām tu sarveṣām saṃkhyādevinaḥ vidyate sarva bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca bināśaḥ mama abhaktānām saṃhāre pina vidyate yaḥ bhūyas devatā yuktaḥ śraddhayā ācaya te naraḥ tasya tām mūrtim āsthāya prasīdāmi na saṃśayaḥ tasya aham na praṇaśyāmi sacamena praṇaśyati sarva ārambha itu yaḥ nityam satatam dhyāna karmaṇā samām praviśate devinā asti tatra vicāraṇā dhattūrakaiḥ ca puṣpaiḥ ca vilva pattraiḥ śva śobhanaiḥ tat karavīra sahasram vā āyām me dadyāt viśeṣataḥ śru arkāṇām tu sahasreṇa padma me kam viśiṣyate campakasya mahābhāge puṣpam dhattūrakaiḥ smṛtam tathā parvasu suśroṇi tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu saṃvatsareṇa ca ekena puṣpāṇām yat phalam labhet śobhanaiḥ divya gandha āṭyaiḥ bhṭaṇu tasya api yat phalam baka puṣpa pradānena aśīti svarṇa jam phalam mahat phalam mahat mama tulyaḥ naraḥ bhūtvā triśūlī vṛṣa vāhanaḥ yaḥ tu śaṃkara nirmālyam pādena ākramate naraḥ ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇi tiryagyoniṣu jāyate tad hanaḥ āsana ādinā yama niyamayoḥ sādhāraṇyāt iti bhāvaḥ padma arcitaiḥ praśasta pāḥ taiḥ samam iti śeṣaḥ tāvat dāna jam bhūtvā ācarati iti śeṣaḥ akāmāt vā akāmāt api iti viṃśatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ traya triṃśat sahasrāṇi deva dānava rākṣasāḥ pūjayantiṃ tumān nityam dharma kāma artha siddhaye akāmāt paṭhate nityam yaḥ ca evam śṛṇu yān naraḥ rudra lokam avāpnoti tuṣṭaḥ tasya vṛṣadhvajaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām puppasamuddeśaḥ nāma viṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca śrotum icchāmi bhagavant yena tuṣyati śaṃkaraḥ puṣpam ca kīdṛśam proktam puṣpa mūlyam tu kīdṛśam kena puṣpeṇa kim puṇyam parimāṇam prakīrtitam teṣām ca kīdṛśam yogam upayuktam mahat phalam yena kena prakāreṇa ārya pūri aśva śaṃkaraḥ mahātmānam mahādevam svayam devī tapas sthitā vijñāpayati deveśam bhūtānām ādim avyayam tvam nātha devadeveśayena tuṣyasi śaṃkaraiḥ etat praśna varam brūhi yathā pṛṣṭa mahā ṛṣibhiḥ uvāca puṣpāṇi rakta pītāni asitāni tathā apare sugandhinaḥ sugandhāḥ cana anāgandhāḥ tathā eva ca teṣām tra saṃkhyām vakṣyāmi devi ekamanāḥ śṛṇu tu durgandhā dānaveṣu ca karkaśāḥ lomaśāḥ ca eva rākṣasāṇām channti caye martyāḥ puṣpāṇi vividhāni ca tepām kīdṛśaḥ dharmaḥ sammārjana upalepane uvāca śṛṇu devi yathātathyam kīrtyamānam idam śṛṇu haktitas asya pradānena bhaktimān īśvare dvijaḥ daśa ca eva sahasrāṇi apsarobhiḥ cakrīḍate tad aśītika avijñeyāḥ māṣāḥ ekādaśā api atha etat devī pramāṇena suvarṇa āśīrti bhaktimān droṇapuṣpaṃca kundam ca kurute śaṃkara arcanam ca sauvarṇikāḥ smṛtāḥ mahīyate tailena api priya udāhṛta abhāve tu mānavaḥ tena dīpa pradānena śaśi vat rājate dvijaḥ puṣpa upahāra dhūpaiḥ ca śatam yoginam uttamam mālā śata sahasrasya japyam śataguṇam smṛtam agarum gandha dhūpam ca candanam ca vilepanam ekaviṃśat suvarṇāni mayāte tam pṛthak trāpayet liṅgam ghṛta abhyaṅgam ca kārayet pitṛ gandharva yakṣāṇām nāgānām rāsām tathā sarva loka hita arthāya mayā ate kīrtitam tathā tathā mad puṣpa vidhiḥ pra uktaḥ svayam īśena vai dvijaiḥ puṣpa ādibhiḥ yoginam sevamānam śataguṇam phalam āmoti iti arthaḥ iti ekaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ namaḥ śivāya dvāviṃśe anāśakaiḥ vidhiḥ nānā aśubha phala āvahaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām ekaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tīrthānām ca eva māsānām vidhānam paramam tathā upaviṣṭāḥ tu deva ādi ākhya ṛkṣa tripura śāsanam deva gandharva sahitā muni saṃgha samākulāḥ praṣṭum ca parameśānam paramam ṛṣi pūjitam pareśaḥ bhagavān indraḥ bhavān agniḥ sanātanaḥ bhavān dharmaśva kāmaśva saṃkalpaśva manīṣiṇaḥ tvam tuṣṭiḥ tvam dhṛtiḥ medhā śraddhā kāmaḥ manaḥ tathā candra arkau na prakāśete yasmin deśe gatā mama mad bhaktāḥ tasmin deśe su tejasā manīṣibhiḥ māhātmyam te sura śreṣṭhayaḥ paṭhet niyataḥ naraḥ hārayiṣyanti ye ca anye śraddadhāna aśva mānavāḥ tepa kilviṣam kiṃcid tvayi tuṣṭe bhaviṣyati akṣayaśva aprameyaśva purāṇapuruṣa uttam tvam vāyuḥ analaḥ ca evam tvam jalam tvam mahī smṛtaḥ mallikā yūthī aśva pañca sauvarṇikāḥ smṛtaḥ raktotpalam tathā ca anye sapta sauvaṇikāḥ smṛtāḥ daśa sauvaṇikā jñeyā bilva aśokam iti smṛtāḥ kesara vṛkṣotpalam tu vijñeyam suvarṇāni tu dvādaśa dvātriṃśat suvarṇāni padma puṣpam atra kīrtitam śivaḥ āha jāti ityādi pañca sauvarṇikāḥ suvarṇapañcaka dāna phalaka arpaṇāḥ evam api bhavati iti śeṣaḥ iti prābhuvanti iti śeṣaḥ māṃchata āyāmayataḥ aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi kuśapuṣpam prakīrtitam dvi sahasam tu vijñeyam śaṃkaram vai nigadyate sahasra aśīti vijñeyam bakapuṣpam nigadyate śatasāhasikaḥ jñeyaḥ dhattūrakaḥ iti smṛtaḥ etāvat puṣpa jātīnām gandham āghrāmi aham sadā aṣṭa etaiḥ puṣpa viśeṣaiḥ su kuryāt nāma arcanam sadā mārga siṃha ārūḍhaiḥ vyāpakam phalam manāḥ pūjayet māntu yonaraḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ ākāśena eva pāśena badhyate brahma vādinaḥ dhāroṣṇena tu kṣīreṇa pūjayitvā mama agratas nivedayet yathākāmam tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu koṭi śata sahasrāḥ tuhimālaye yatra tatra yathā tathā sarveṣām ca eva puṣpāṇām viśeṣeṇa upalabhyate sa balā devadārum vā abhaktyā dhūpam pradāpayet śiva arcanam praśaṃsati mahātmānaḥ api muni yātanaiḥ munīnām api yātanā tad sthānī tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu dvātriṃśat tu suvarṇāni sārdha aśīti punar punar ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇi modatecama mālaye kāla dīpaṃtamaḥ dadyāt saṃvatsaram mama api cam hṛdaya stham śivaḥ ca eva bhaktānām tu sureśvaraḥ yavas haste suraśreṣṭhaiḥ sarva bhūta namaskṛtaḥ aṣṭau kāmān prayacchasva akṣayāni mahāmate tvam gatiḥ sarva bhūtānām śaraṇam tvam na saṃśayaḥ ṛṣibhiḥ strāpayet ha maṃlabhate mahatīm śriyam bhava pārśvam upāgamya prāñjaliḥ prayata ākaraiḥ upavāsam param dharma spṛśanti manasā a smṛtāḥ sarveṣām eva varṇān na kim phalam labhate naraḥ śrī mahādevaḥ uvāca haṇude vi yathānyāyam upavāsa phalam śubham yathā ca vālakhilyānām naimiṣa araṇya vāsinām upavāsa phalam divyam samṛddhānām daridrāṇām jantūnām duḥkha jīvinām mita tvena mama vatrāt viśeṣataḥ mokṣam vā api viśeṣataḥ sarvam etat aśeṣeṇa pravakṣyāmi anupūrvaśas yathā api devi saṃproktāḥ tathā tu ekamanāḥ śṛṇu pañcamī ca eva ṣaṣṭhī ca paurṇamāsī tathā eva ca upoṣya āmama bhaktena piyat phalam subhagā udarśanīya śva jñāna bhāgībhaviṣyati tathā eva ca aṣṭamī bhavet upoṣyā eka rātreṇa bhṭaṇutasya api yat phalam vasu āḍhyaḥ bahu putra śva vidyā bhāgī ca jāyate śuklām caturdaśīm ca eva yāvat śukla aṣṭamī bhavet upoṣyāḥ eka rātreṇa syāpi yat phalam subhaga udarśanīya śva jñāna bhāgībhavet naraḥ nāṭyaḥ ca bahu putraḥ bhavet naraḥ dvādaśyām tu sadā vyāsaḥ eka bhaktena pūjayet hi vidyā bhāgī dhana avyaśca dhana bhāgī tu nirdiśet tri rātreṇa yaḥ tu saṃvatsaram kṣipet mahīyate māse māse trirātreṇa yaḥ tu saṃvatsaram kṣipet apsaras gaṇa saṃghṛṣṭā ivi mānedivi rājate tu kārttike ca vicakṣaṇaḥ apaḥ ca eva pivet māsam nivṛttaḥ bhojana antare pauṣa māsam mahābhāge tasya api tvam vidhim śṛṇu ca śaktyā tu dakṣiṇām dadyāt śṛṇutasya api yat phalam mahātmānaḥ śubhān lokān sarvadevena vanditāḥ śata varṣa sahasrāṇām sukham santi ca tri rātram kṣapayet yaḥ tu māgha imā setu yonaraḥ vividhena anna pānena tarpayitvā tu brāhmaṇān śaktitas dakṣiṇām dadyāt śṛṇutasya api yat phalam ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇi triṃśat varṣa śatāni ca bhāgaśas sarveṣām eva sammānam rājarājena pūjitaḥ bhālgunam tu yadā māsam eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣipet tasya śaktitas dakṣiṇām dayāt śṛṇutasya api yat phalam jñāna vijñāna saṃpanna avinīta aśva bhavanti te dharma jñāḥ ca su bhāryā śva aneka kratu yājakāḥ caitra māsam mahābhāge eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣipet tasmin māse samāpte tu pūjayitvā tumāṃpriye vidhinā annena pānena tarpayitvā tu brāhmaṇān mahatyā tu dakṣiṇām dayāt śṛṇutasya api yat phalam aśītim tu sahasrāṇi śata varṣāṇi pañca yat vāruṇam lokam āpnoti yā nena mama tejasā vaiśākham tu yadā māsam eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣipet tasmin māse samāpte tu pūjayitvā tumāṃpriye vidhinā annena pānena tarpayitvā tu brāhmaṇān mahatyā tu dakṣiṇām dayāt śṛṇutasya api yat phalam triṃśat varṣa sahasrāṇi svarga loke mahīyate tatas vāpī cyutaḥ bhūyas gavām koṭi pradaḥ bhavet ca eka bhaktam mad bhaktena antarātmanā tasmin māse samāpte tu pūjayitvā tumāṃpriye vidhinā anne na pānena tarpayitvā ca brāhmaṇān na teṣām punarāvṛttiḥ vidyate tu mahātmanām ha epa īśvara sambhāvaḥ kathitaḥ te samāsatas upavāsasya yat puṇyam sāṃvatsaram yathā uditam sārvakāmikam akṣayyam pitṛbhyaḥ vā upatiṣṭhati ca eva kapilām yaśca dadyāt ekasya brāhmaṇaḥ mad mad prabhāvāt prabhāvaḥ sām labhate ekaviṃśati kalpāni jātim evam na na āpnuyāt na jahāti ca tam dharma rāja dharma samāśritaḥ āṣāḍha māse saptamyām eka bhakta upoṣitaḥ āsthitaḥ labhate bahuśas dharma yoti upoṣati ca aṣṭamīm hrāvaṇam tu yadā vyāsaiḥ eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣipet vividha annena pānena tarpayitvā ca brāhmaṇān tu dakṣiṇām dadyāt śṛṇutasya api yatkam pitaraḥ tasya tuṣyanti viṃśat varṣa śatāni ca jñātvā ca brāhmaṇān śaktyā tu dakṣiṇām dadyāt śṛṇutasya api yat phalam mahīyate tad pramāṇena catur veda adhyāpanīya śvayaḥ bhavet māsvinam tu yadā vyāsaḥ eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣipet tu dakṣiṇām dayāt śṛṇutasya api yat phalam mahīyate medhāvī vīrya saṃpannaḥ dhanībhavati mānavaḥ kīrtitam aṣṭa varṣasya kālasya pañcadhā sa bhavet naraḥ mama bhakti ratānām ca ekānta ra upavāsinām pakṣa upavāsinām ca eva tathā māsa upavāsinām hasa ambu bhakṣāṇām vaset tu jala śāyinām brahmacāri vratānām ca phala mūla āśinām tathā evaṃvidham pravakṣyāmi śṛṇutasya api yat phalam yaḥ tu kalyam ca sāyam ca bhuṃjānaḥ na antaram pivet ahiṃsā nirataḥ ca eva śṛṇutasya api yat phalam pauṇḍarīkasya yajñasya phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ ahiṃsā nirataḥ ca eva śṭaṇutasya api yat phalam prāyas tad āyuḥ ca eva jāyate yaḥ tu dvādaśa varṣāṇi eka āhāraḥ bhavet naraḥ ahiṃsā nirataḥ ca eva śṛṇutasya api yat phalam hi śata varṣa sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭi varṣa śatāni ca pade pade yajña phalam labhate ca anupūrvaśas kām cīnūpura śabde vasoḥ saṃpratibuddhyate mṛdaṅga veṇu śabdena vaṃśaiḥ adhruvam utthitaḥ prātar vīrāsanam araṇya cāri tva ādikam divasam pañcaśatikam rātrau sāhasikam japet balavān rūpa saṃpannaḥ labhate vipulām śriyam dīpa pradānam yaḥ udayāt daivate trāhmaṇeṣu ca atas ūrdhva pravakṣyāmi śṛṇutasya api yat phalam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ dadāti iha pānīyam śraddhayā anvitaḥ candra pradānam yaḥ dadyāt dijāya jvalitāni ca dhenu pradānam yaḥ dayāt rāhmaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ yāvanti romakūpāni tasya ā gātreṣu tiṣṭhati rūpavān śīla saṃpannaḥ vidyāvān śru bhavet naraḥ vastra dānam ca yaḥ dadyāt rāhmaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ kapilā dānam yaḥ dadyāt rāhmaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ yāvanti romakūpāṇi tat syāḥ gātreṣu vai dvija kanyā dānam tu yad udayāt rāhmaṇebhyaḥ viśeṣataḥ brāhmaṇānām vivāhe ca vidhinā dvijasattamaiḥ śayyā pradānam yaḥ udayāt rāhmaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ paṣṭi varṣa sahasrāṇi svarga loke mahīyate yat tudānam mayā avyāsa tavastre hāt udīritam upavāsasya yat puṇyam sāram ca eva sanātanam iti dvāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ mad namaḥ śivāya trayoviṃśe śiva prīti kārakaḥ dharma auttamaḥ tad bahu dharma samāśritya ahiṃsāḥ satya vādinaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām upa vāsavidhiḥ nāma dvāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tryakṣa tribhuvana śreṣṭha tryambaka tridaśeśvara yakṣa rakṣaḥ pramathana śūlapāṇe ripuṃjaya ca eva anāśakaḥ paricaryā niyamāḥ yamāḥ katham puṣpāṇi gandhāni phalāni kim svid syāt prabrūhi deveśvara śūlapāṇe śrī mahādevaḥ uvāca caturdaśīm aṣṭamī camat bhakta uyaḥ kṣipet naraḥ aṣṭamyām tuvarāraḥ hegavām snāpayet ca nirāhāraḥ prasanna ātmā ajita indriyaḥ devasya utpādanam kṛtvā amunā avividhāḥ kriyāḥ siddha mantram sādhayeta śāka mūla phalāni ca caturvidhāyām mṛta tu sthaṃḍila eva ciṃtayet jānubhyām jānunā avāpi udbhūta rasāṃni ca tasya aham na eva tuṣya abhivimukhaḥ aham varānane mantram ca eva pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣva āyata locane tam aham puṃḍarīkākṣam rudram om kārayāmi aham āyāntu devāḥ sa gaṇāḥ umā devī maheśvarī bhagavante mahādevāya pārśva gatāya anucarāya svāhā malakam sūkṣmam a yam śivaḥ trānam punar bhajasvāhā taiḥ sarvam eva umā yute svāhā imāḥ āpaḥ śāntāḥ śatitamāḥ aṣṭatāḥ amṛtatamāḥ āpaḥpūtāḥ brahma pavitreṇa pūtāḥ sūryasya raśmibhiḥ āṃ hāraḥ sarva davānām gandhaḥ ayam pratigṛhyatām svāhā su gandham sumanaḥ divyaiḥ sarva gandhaiḥ alaṃkṛtam pūtam brahma pavitreṇa pūtam sūryasya raśmibhiḥ puṣpam dattam mayā bhaktyā pratigṛhṇa namaḥ astu te namaḥ prajānām pataye namaḥ bhakta gaṇa ācitaiḥ tigṛhla emam dhūpam śiva liṅga namaḥ stute svāhā māṃ prabhavaḥ smṛtaḥ pūtaḥ brahma pavitreṇa pūtaḥ sūryasya raśmibhiḥ mama idam dīpam śiva liṃga namaḥ stu te nivedya manasā yuktam devānām gandham uttamam pūtaḥ trahma pavitreṇa pūtaḥ sūryasya raśmibhiḥ svāhā arcitaḥ pūjitaḥ ca eva mayā abhaktyā api apūjitaḥ dhanavān api jyeṣṭham āsam kṣipet yaḥ vai eka bhaktam samācaran xchaḥ bhavatiḥ bhrātṝṇām bhogān āpnoti puṣkalān māsam eka bhaktam samācaret sa rājñaḥ mānyatām prāpya kāmān āpnoti puṣkalān māse eka bhaktam samācaret saināpatyam ca saṃprāpya balavān apijāyate yā api ca āśvayujam māsam eka bhaktena tiṣṭhati ha vāṇijyam labhate tasya kṛṣiḥ paśu gaṇāḥ tathā tiṣṭhati yaḥ kṣipet eka bhaktena bhum kte divase ṣaṣṭhe nityam niyamam āsthitaḥ āsādya saca videt aṣṭame ahani yaḥ bhuṃkte pratimāsam atandritaḥ vāruṇam lokam āsthāya saca videt mahat phalam tat sūryaḥ sadā mānuṣyam ca punar prāpya daśa bhāryā labheta saḥ ekādaśe tu yoḥ bhukte divase mānavaḥ śuciḥ ekādaśyāḥ phalam prāpya yajñavān iha jāyate atha iha mānuṣaḥ bhūtvā sanaraḥ jāyate śuciḥ iha rājā mahān bhūmau yatra tatra abhijāyate athavā a hu tvāni asamāhitaḥ dīkṣayitvā tathā ātmānam upavāsam caret dijaḥ tam yānti śaraṇam ca eva durgam pāla agniḥ eva ca yaḥ japan devagāyatrīm pavitrāṇi ca nityaśas rudra nāma guṇān vāpī rātri auca sthaṇḍileśayaḥ kuśān āstīrya vidhivat strī śūdra parivarjitaḥ samaśnīyāt tu vairātrau vīta rāgaḥ vimatsaraḥ yāvati ahāni saṃtiṣṭhet tāvat viprān tu bhojayet tatas pūrṇe tu kāle vai brāhmaṇānām tila pātrāṇi yaḥ dadyāt viprebhyaḥ śraddhayā naraḥ tad amāvā syāṃsa māsa agra kṛṣṇa aṣṭamī samāhitaḥ yaḥ tu cāndrāyaṇam kuryāt yathā ukta mu samāhitaḥ tarpayitvā tu akṣayam nara puṃga vaḥ pavitrāṇām vidhim bhū yaḥ ekacittā avadhāya mahā sāṃtapanam yaḥ tu karoti su mahāmanāḥ tulāpuruṣa kaṃya śvāti dvijasattame avāpnuyāt śrva sarvāṇi dānāni kurute nara sattamaḥ yam yam prārthayate kāmam tam tam eva samaśnute tam ca upayuñjānaḥ go mūtreṇa apisaṃskṛtam piṇyāka mātra bhakṣaḥ vā vāyubhakṣaḥ yava apunar yā vat uktam samāsena mahātmā anaṣṭa kilviṣaḥ sālokyam vā mahā śabdam yatheṣṭam mokṣam eva ca tat dṛśyate niyamānām ca yoga dhyāna tapas layāḥ eṣa mama saṃśayaḥ deva citta vyākula kārakaḥ mahābuddhe nīhāram iva bhāskaraḥ śrī maheśvaraḥ uvāca niyamam tu naraḥ kṛtvā niyamāt niyata indriyaḥ duṣkaram niyamam kartu manuṣyeṇa viśeṣataḥ mahiṃsakāḥ deva tva devatāḥ prāptāḥ aniyamāt niyama anvite maṃca yathā tathā mama patnī tvam āyāsi tvam śubhena atra saṃśayaḥ māse ca niyamam yaḥ ca kurute niyamān tatas dvijātīnām priyam tat me niśāmaya naga ātmaje niṣṭhuraḥ karuṇaḥ devī jāti karma vighaṭṭakaḥ tyāṃdhrajaḥ pāpaḥ aviśuddhaḥ bhāti matsaraḥ mithyā vinītaḥ durmedhā deva dānava dhikkṛtaḥ para dravyeṇa saṃtuṣṭaḥ para dravya avicārakaḥ uddejanīyaḥ sarvasya duṣṭa ahiḥ iva pārvati mithyā vinītaḥ durmedhāḥ veda vāda vahiṣkṛtaḥ chinna daṃṣṭraḥ yathā sarpaḥ śṛṅga hīnaḥ yathā vṛṣaḥ nunna pakṣaḥ yathā pakṣi vipuṣpā eva pādapaḥ vārāṇasyām sarvaiḥ vipraḥ vipra koṭi śata ardanaḥ āste sma śatapattra akṣi solasa vā artha hārakaḥ tasyām puryāṇa saḥ asti iha puruṣaḥ pramadā uttame yasya iṣṭaḥ sa bhavet bhīruḥ duṣṭa ahiḥ iva duḥkha daḥ tam rucira ānane tasya varṣa śatāni eva vaṇij āpaṇagasya vai pārvati atha ambu japa daḥ siddhaḥ siddha gandharva pūjitaḥ vārāṇasīm gataḥ draṣṭum oṃkāram siddha rāhmaṇa ṛṣabha rambhām anāmayam pṛccha vacanāt mama sattamaiḥ apakrāman divam kāntām vāyuḥ avyāhataḥ yathā apaśyat suka tīram bhām bhraṣṭa padmām iva śriyam pūrṇa candra ābha vadanām madana aṅga mayām dṛṣṭvā anavadyāṅgām idam vacanam abravīt nivasati brāhmaṇaḥ hi vai rāṃgane sa tvā pṛcchati suśroṇi yadi jānāsi kathyatām uvāca he anuprāptaḥ dvijātinā ca saṃpṛṣṭaḥ śvireṇa punar āgataḥ satam prahasya provāca vārāṇasyām niketanaḥ brāhmaṇa dṛṣṭā asā tvayā āraṃbhā vara apsarāḥ ha kāni sā avadate dṛṣṭā pṛcchatā iva asura aṅganā rambhā dṛṣṭā tatas te prahasya vacanāt mama vyaśālinī atha saḥ eva siddhaḥ svargāt punar kāśyām samāgataḥ te ciram vicintya mām āha na eva jānāmi kaḥ pi asau uvāca brāhmaṇaḥ asmi punar svargam yadā anāma mahā dyute svarge sukṛtinām vāse saṃgataḥ uraṃbhayā ca saḥ sa arambhā sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām aṣṭāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tad viṣa doṣa phalam śrutvā girīśa tanayā avyayā āśā vasana deva īśanā asti dhanyatarā amayā bhūtyā aparayā ayuktam bhūtyā ca su vibhūṣitam paśyāmi tvā abhisaṃnibhām candra ābhe candra vada necaṃdra paṅkaja hāsini śṛṇu devi yathā bhūtiḥ vilepanam abhūt mama tad brahmanaḥ bhṛgu vaṃśe prabhāvāt iva māsya āyatana apavipulaṃtapaḥ hemante ca jaleśayaḥ
