krama viśeṣeṇa yogānām lakṣaṇam param pravakṣyāmi yathātattvam svayam rudreṇa bhāṣitam prāṇāyāmaḥ tathā ca api prāṇasyāyāmaḥ ucyate mātrāḥ ṣaṭtriṃśatiḥ smṛtāḥ iti eṣa vividhaḥ proktaḥ prāṇāyāmasya lakṣaṇaḥ vane te yogam niviśamānaḥ tu na doṣam prāpnuyāt kvacid yamāna yogasya tathā jāyeta mārutaḥ ca tathā ca api gacchate yogam āsthitaḥ yathā siṃhaḥ mṛga go vāpī nīyamānaḥ vyavasthitaḥ abhayam ca manuṣyāṇām mṭagebhyaḥ saṃpravartate mārutaḥ yoginaḥ vaśyaḥ bhavati iti bhāvaḥ vyavasthitaḥ vaṃśe sthitaḥ bhavati iti śeṣaḥ manasipī vāyām casamaḥ viṣaya antaram bhāvaḥ sīvanyāḥ vṛṣaṇa madhya ga rekhāyāḥ tathā a paricīyamānaḥ śarīra kilbiṣam dehat prāṇāyāmena yuktasya viprasya niyata ātmanaḥ sarva doṣāḥ praṇaśyaṃti sattva sthaḥ ca eva jāyate tīrthāni yāni paṭhyante niyamāni tratāni ca taiḥ taiḥ dahet doṣān dhāraṇābhiḥ sva kilbiṣam pratyāhāreṇa viṣayān dhyānena anaśvarān guṇān tasmāt yuktaḥ sadā yogī prāṇāyāḥ mām samācaret atas param pravakṣyāmi prāṇāyāmasya lakṣaṇam āsanam svastikam kuryāt padyam bhadrāsanam tathā sama jānum eka pāda pāṇi ottānam ca saṃsthitaḥ manas grīvā samas bhu tva saṃgṛ tya caraṇau ubhau jā jā nṛ varaṃtare vipra kṛtvā pāda tale aṅguṣṭhau api gṛhṇīyāt hastābhyām vyutkrameṇa tu kṣiṣ pārśva pāda ca pāṇibhyām dṛḍha badhvā su niśvalaḥ saṃvṛta āsyaḥ umīlita akṣa upaviṣṭa śva vāgyataḥ pāṇibhyām dapaṇam rakṣet tathā śephena nityaśas datta anna saṃspṛśet jivhām na cālayet kvāpi pāṣāṇa eva niśvalaḥ sthiraḥ yogī saṃyuktaḥ su samāhitaḥ tad tad indriyāṇi indriya arthaḥ ca manas pañcama vāyavaḥ ma bhāvena kūrma ūgāni iva sarvaśas nivṛtti viṣayāṇām tu pratyāhāram upakramet tathā dvādaśa mātraḥ tu prāṇāyāmaḥ vidhīyate dhāraṇā dvādaśāyām īsevet ca dhāraṇātyayam daśa dvādaśa viṃśatyā catu viṃśati dhāraṇāḥ dhāraṇā ādhārayet yogī nityam adhyātma citakaḥ paśyate paramātmānam divyam evam kutas janiḥ dhārayitvā ayathāśaktyā aśanaiḥ pratyāharet punar hi jitvā a jitvā aśanaiḥ bhūyas ārabhet ca sadā muniḥ atha vivardhayati saṃmūḍham tasmāt eva jitā a mahī prāṇāyāmasya saṃrodhāt prāṇāyāmaḥ tu paṭhyate dhārayet ca api yat vāyuṃdhāraṇām iti nirdiśet nivatta viṣayāṇām tu pratyāhāram na saṃśayaḥ sarveṣām samavāyena siddhiḥ syāt yoga lakṣaṇā mad dhyāna yuktāḥ tu paśyaṃti ātmānam jala caṃdra vat tathā a saṃdarśanam prāpte kṣema prāpti vinirdiśet deśa kāla videśaḥ tam vijñeyam tattva lakṣaṇam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām yogavidhiḥ nāma trayastriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca sukha upaviṣṭam āsīnam mahādevam svayambhum papraccha muni śārdūlaḥ durvāsāḥ tu mahā muniḥ bhagavantam bhava udvignā edam āha ruta añjaliḥ bhagavan kena mucyate narāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca eva tathā vibho mleccha mātaṃgāḥ śūkarāḥ pakṣi ghātakāḥ pāpa āśrayāḥ lolupāḥ ca havirdhakāḥ tasyāḥ dūṣakāḥ ca eva kula ghnāḥ strī napuṃsakāḥ mātṛtyāgī piṭatyāgī rāja ghnāḥ ca eva ye narāḥ para dravya apahārīca yuddhe ca api parāṅmukhāḥ aśaktau aṅkuśaḥ ca eva śakti āvṛtti bhuja śvaye matsya vaddhāśva agamyāgama neratāḥ ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ sarva pāpeṣu ye narāḥ gacchan tena katham tāta pāpiṣṭhām gatim eva ca brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca eva tathā apare mleccha mātaṃgāya ca anye pāpa karmiṇaḥ evam evam te dhyāninaḥ viprāḥ date pāpa kaṃkṣaṇāt pitṛ patnī bhrātṛ patnīm bhagi nīm gāvam eva ca dhyāninām śuddha buddhīnām dhyānena vidita ātmanām dhyānam ciṃtayamānasya ekacittena dhyāninaḥ ekena dhyāna yogena tad pāpam nirdahet kṣaṇāt vaca saṃśayaḥ dhyāna hīnaḥ yaḥ tu nityam dṛḍha yuktaḥ dṛḍha vrataḥ agni lokam vāyu lokam indra lokam prajāpatiḥ viṣṇu loka antaram gatvā brahma lokāt parām gatim iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tathā etat icchāmi aham śrotum tvad prasādāḥ dravīhi me aham vakṣyāmi tat sarva śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ mama oṃkāram paramam dhyānam yogam yuṃjīta yoga vid upaviśya āsanam tatra soma maṇḍalakam tathā padma maṇḍalakam ca eva svastikaṃsam udāhṛtam mahā rudra poṭhaṃcavacaṃcavajjadaṃḍoṃ nnataṃ tathā iti ete āsanāḥ proktāḥ nānā rūpa guṇa anvitāḥ eteṣām ekam āsthāya āsanam tu vicakṣaṇaḥ tad patiḥ bhūtvā rudra ādi lokān gacchati iti arthaḥ iti catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ maḥ śivāya paṃcatriṃśattame adhyāye ladhu āhāra ujita krodha ekānte ca nirāmayaḥ maṃsta saṃsarga vai jitve darśana abhyāgamam tathā ciṃtaya īḍya āninaḥ nityam śāstra dṛṣṭe na karmaṇā ekāgra mānasaḥ bhūtvā utpattim pralayam tathā yuṃjīta sva śarīrasya yum jānona ca hiṃsakaḥ yathā hi aham śarīrasya śukra śoṇita saṃbhavaḥ kim naḥ śarīra arthe anitye ca eva śarīrake majjā medas sthi saṃpūrṇa sirā jālena saṃvṛte mūtra purīṣe pudurgandha janma sambhave mamatvam śoka gaṇe ghoram ke prāṇāḥ tu rudraiḥ avijñeyāḥ avimuktam param smṛtam hita artham sarva jantuṣu antaram śṛṇuyāt yogam yogaviyam varam sadā manaḥ tvac cakṣuṣī jivhā nāsikā ca iti pañcamī mahābhūtāni kartavyam jñāna artha jñānam eva ca avyaktam parisaṃkhyātum prāṇāyāmaḥ tu dhāraṇā prāṇāyāmaiḥ vaśaṃkṛtvā sarvām indriya vāhinīm tatas yuṃjīta medhāvī prāṇam ca manasā muniḥ pṛthak bhāvanā tattvānām paśu ākuñjīta mūrdhani ekatvam prāṇa manasaḥ indriyāṇām samanvitaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumāra saṃhitāyām sanatkumāra saṃhitāyām durvāsa upanipad nāma pañcatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ amanasā iti pañca triśaḥ adhyāyaḥ prāṇa upānaḥ samānaḥ udānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca tān hitvā vāyavaḥ paṃca dhārayaṃti ātmanā ātmani bhāde ca eva ūru jaṅghā suśilā vṛṣaṇayoḥ tathā pāyu upastha kaṭī vā avhoḥ hṛdaye pārśvayoḥ tathā ye vipule madhye pṛṣṭhe ca atha lalāṭayoḥ nābhi madhye śarīrasya viditam sūrya maṇḍalam mālā sahasā aiḥ tu āpyamāna ipu tejasā tad soma maṇḍalam adhyetu paramātmā abhitiṣṭhati asthi snāyu śirā māṃsa varjita aduḥkha varjitaḥ tad tad ca śyāmaḥ naca raktaḥ naca kṛṣṇaḥ naca pāṇḍuraḥ tat tat tat tat tat tat ca lohitonanaśābalaḥ hi āditya varṇa puruṣam satam vidyāt vicakṣaṇaḥ bhavaḥ ca eva cityaḥ kartā asa kīrtyate tad śuddha sphaṭika varṇa ābhaḥ dṛśyate na ca cakṣuṣā krīḍā artha sṛjate lokān khyāti arthe ca maheśvaraḥ loke pu krīḍate nityam vālaḥ krīḍanakaiḥ iva thā pattram sarva vyāptam hi tantubhiḥ tiṣṭhati sūrya iraśmiḥ yayā atyeṣa sarva tejāṃsi dhāraya evam tena tathā vyānam śarīram paramātmanā paramātmā iti vijñeyaḥ jñāna abhyāsena bho dvijaiḥ abhyāsāt paśyate sarvam paramā ātmānam ātmani na imam yoga vidhiḥ utvā śṭaṇu tattvam manīṣiṇaḥ daśa prāṇa vahāḥ nāḍyaḥ dehi deha iṣu saṃsthitāḥ catasraḥ vastu vijñeyāt decanā āḍhya ūca pārśvayoḥ mūrdhvam tu caturaḥ jñeyāḥ nāḍyaḥ tu parikīrtitāḥ nāḍīnām tu sahasrāṇi dvāsaptatiḥ iti padma saṃkāśa saṃsthānam hṛdayam tatra dṛśyate sūkṣmaḥ hi puruṣaḥ jñeyaḥ parātmā hṛdisaṃsthitaḥ m tvam savaga iṣu sarva gāmī tīrtha sraṣṭā dhātā ca prayuktavan prasūtaḥ thita abhāvānām traṣṭā āhartā aprasavitā adharma utsukaḥ tat eva agniḥ tat ādityaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca jñāpayāmi punar deva prasādam kuru śam kara kīdṛśaḥ utha bhavet dehe ṣaṣ aṅgaḥ yogaḥ ucyate prāṇāyāmaḥ tathā dhyānam dhāraṇā yogaḥ ucyate prāṇasya grahaṇam nityam prāṇāyāmaḥ saḥ ucyate oṃkāram manasā adhyāyet ekāgre manasā a smaran dhyānena tu sadā yogī dhyāna saṃvitta tā paraḥ sarveṣām idriyāṇām tu viṣayāṇām tathā eva ca tat saḥ ucyate daśānām indriyāṇām tu oṃkāra prīta mānasaḥ maṃcamam brahmacarya ca eti ete niyamāḥ smṛtāḥ akrodhaḥ guru śuśrūṣā śaucam saṃtoṣam ṛya vat ete tu niyamāḥ pañca vijñeyāḥ brahma vādiṣu tad eva śuddhevijñānā ucyate saḥ gacchet paramam sthānam śāśvatam padam avyayam tu śūnyam tu yasya arthe śarīram kīrtitam budhaiḥ sa śarīraḥ saḥ ucyate jñānam nirañjanam ca eva avyaktam triguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ tathā eva ca puruṣam śāśvatam sūkṣmam draṣṭavyam dhyāna cakṣuṣā avyaktam triguṇam bhadrapuruṣa śvātra śāśvataḥ pañcaviṃśatī tu vijñeyam īśam īśāḥ nam avyayam sambhūtim ca vināśam ca bhāva abhāvau tathā eva ca yaḥ tu vetti naraḥ prājñaḥ sarve draṣṭā aṣṭaviṃśakaḥ pañcaviṃśaka tattvāni jñāyaṃte tu sadā naraiḥ pañcaviśatī tadā jñeyam īśānam avyayam param puruṣaḥ saṃca ditvā ca jñātvā ca sa gacchet paramām gatim saḥ evam pañcaviṃśatikaḥ ṣaḍūiṃśakaḥ tathā eva ca mad ūnaviṃśatikam vidyāt tatva jñāna artha cintakaḥ tat ājñātvā amṛta tvāya kalpate caturviṃśa gṛhaṃyogaḥ eṣa vai pañcaviṃśakaḥ tathā jñe yā adhyakṣaḥ saptaviṃśakaḥ aṣṭaviṃśakaḥ puruṣaḥ triṃśat puruṣa loka dhṛk yam yam viditvā na śocanti tam śivam kathayāmi te om kāram paramam devam paṃ ca āyatana vāsinam uvāca katham jñeyam hi bhagavat mātra akṣara vivarjitam mātra akṣara vivarjitam yatiḥ mālinī tṛtīyā animiṣā ca eva vijñeyā yoga citakaiḥ mātrā vai vijñeyā aguṇa varjitā ca eva ca eva tām viditvā atum ucyate akāraḥ tāca eva aukāra ukṣara gāminī makāraḥ miṣa anāma praśāntam tupi pīḍitā kāraḥ tu umā ajñeya apraśāntam śāśvatam dhruvam samudāharet vijñāna ākhyāta da ajñeya anityam akṣara gā nidarśanaiḥ iṣukāraḥ iva āsaktaḥ yathā agnim na tu paśyati tādṛśambhāvayet rahma tadā viṃdati tatparam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām durvāsa upaniṣatsu saptatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ idam śarīram vipra indra sarva deva mayam śṛṇu jaṅghayoḥ marutaḥ tathā xchā jānubhyām aśvinaḥ jñeyau ūrubhyām varuṇaḥ tathā om namaḥ śivāya om namaḥ śivāya sarva deva mayam vai ante samudrā vipreṃdra udare pañca deva tāḥ romakūpe dharmaḥ eva mūrdhya ādityaḥ na saṃśayaḥ saṃdhi sama ṛṣayaḥ jñeyāḥ cakṣubhyam sūryaḥ eva ca śrotrāṇi ca diśaḥ sarvā a vijñeyā brahma vādibhiḥ mahā bhūḥ vijñeyaḥ nityam eva pratiṣṭhitaḥ aparāṃteyamaḥ ca eva tathā vedhāḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ pārśvayoḥ madhye prāṇa gatiḥ kaṇṭhe bhavanti vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ etat jñātvā ca paramām gatim uvāca ete proktāḥ śarīrasya adevatāḥ ṛṣayaḥ tathā prāṇa āhutim katham bhante vṛṣabhadhvajaiḥ uvāca prāṇa upānaḥ samāna śvaḥ udānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca iti ete vāyavaḥ pañca śarīra ica pratiṣṭhitāḥ sāvitrī caturaḥ vedāḥ sa paḍaṅga padakramāḥ oṣadhi aśva vanaspatyaḥ soma bhāskara mārutāḥ tena annena tu tṛpyaṃti yat prāṇe juvati dvijāḥ tena nāgāḥ samudra aśva saritaḥ sāgarāḥ tathā ṛṣayaḥ pitaraḥ ca eva sarve devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ samāne juhute yaḥ tu tṛtīyām āhutim dijaḥ aśvinaḥ marutaḥ viṣṇuḥ varuṇaḥ ca yamaḥ tathā prajāpatiḥ kubera śva sarve deva gaṇāḥ tathā tena aham cabhavaḥ bhaunandī gaṇeśvaraḥ umā brahma api vipra indra manaḥprāṇāḥ tathā eva ca māhutim dvi jaḥ sapta loka aśva brahmāṇḍāḥ sa yakṣa uraga rākṣasāḥ rudraḥ evam tu satatam viprāḥ juhute praṇave nave māsasya api bhuṃjānaḥ ūnasa pāpena lipyate brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ yat iva a paṭhet veda aham etam puruṣam mahantam āditya varṇa tamasaḥ parastāt āpnuyāt etam evam idam jñātvā amṛta tvam avāpnuyāt iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām durvāsa upaniṣatsu aṣṭatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca yat tvayā uktam bhagavatā asāṃkhya yoga viśārada yoga nāḍīm imām tra śrotum icchāmi tat vratam praṇamya śirasā devam akṣayam bhuvana īśvaram kātyāyanīm namaskṛtvā rudra patnīm viśeṣataḥ pārameṣṭhyam idam jñānam nāḍī saṃcāra saṃsthitam yadā śrīmān dehasyaḥ krīḍate tadā anantā raśmayaḥ tasya jagat deha āśritāḥ tathā yoga nāḍīḥ pravakṣyāmi hṛdaya sthānam ā śritāḥ pūrva dakṣiṇa paśu ardha auttarām mūrtim āśritāḥ adhastāt deva nāḍyaḥ tu tāsām varṇān nibodha mama pīta lohita kṛṣṇa aśravaḥ uttarāḥ pāṇḍu piṅgalāḥ pūrvāḥ śvetāḥ tathā nāḍyaḥ dakṣiṇāḥ kṛṣṇa piṅgalāḥ hasta tu sthitāyāḥ tu kṛṣṇā nāḍyaḥ tu coditāḥ madhya madhya saṃsthāna saṃśritāḥ śatam eka uttaram nāḍīm upāsate ca yoginaḥ sarva aśva tāḥ samutsṛjya brahma nāḍīm samāśrayet nābhināḍībhiḥ rati artha krīḍā moha visarjanam ṣaṇṇavatayaḥ sahasrāṇi nāḍīnām hṛdi saṃsthitāḥ pūrva nāḍyaḥ tu yāḥ pañca prāṇa ādyāḥ parikītitāḥ dakṣiṇāyāḥ sthitāḥ nāḍyaḥ tāsām pañca jalāḥ iti tu udānam ca uttarāṇi ca samāśritāḥ dviguṇam tu praviṣṭāḥ tu hṛdaya anantaram tatāḥ etat nāḍī pramāṇam tu viśvam yatra pratiṣṭhitam tāḥ caturbhiḥ saṃyuktam aṇoḥ aṇīyānāḍī iti adhastāt saḥ tu viśvakarmaṇā tena eva nāḍhī antara saṃcareṇa śuddhasya nāḍi diśi mūrdhani lakṣayet tad parāpara jñāna nidhāna bhūtāḥ pañca indriyāḥ saṃyuktā pañcakarmabhiḥ indriyaiḥ sarve te hṛdisaṃvaddhā yogena hṛdi pādayoḥ nāḍī sahasrāṇām guṇān eva catuṣṭayam tāḥ ca mūtra vahā nāḍī ekī bhūtātu miśray retasā asaṃprasūyam te mūtram ca eva tathā eva ca brahmanāḍī mukheyasya manasā athṛdica īśvaram trīṇi ca asthi sahasrāṇi varṇa sṛṣṭiḥ prakīrtitā snāyūnām sahasrāṇi param saṃvatsaram smṛtam sūkṣmāt sūkṣmataraḥ bhāvaḥ yam viditvā an ayujyate soma sūrya aṃśubhiḥ pītam padmam ca eva sa vindati tatra upari nayanti eva yoginām mūrdhniśāyinām manasā vijñāya nivṛtta kalmaṣāḥ abhitvā sthitim trahma vidaḥ prayām sanatkumāreṇa idam tu nāḍī saṃcāra sūcitam yoga śāstram idam puṇyam mokṣa śāstram su niśvitam brahma ādyaiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ gatam yoga śāstram viniścitam puṇyāt puṇyataraṃsi etat pavi pāpa nāśanam pramucyate nāḍī madhya gatam viśvam śudhyate pitṛ mātṛ jam go mūtram saptame pāpam dahate ca aṣṭame tathā tena apiśraṅgyā nāḍī mūrdhani adhastāt vi niḥsṛtā mantavyaḥ yena viśvam hṛdi trajet pūrvāḥ te iti aditiṣṭhati tad manas tad parāyaṇāḥ tāvat saṃcita yet ugram yāvatā a tad mataḥ mataḥ nāḍī sūkṣmeṇa mārgeṇa aurdhvayā ati uttarāyaṇam tābhyām adhastāt yat kāryam tat gatam tasya saṃsmṛtam madhyam ca eva nāḍyāḥ tu śarīreyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ snāyuḥ trīṇi sahasrāṇi sarvāḥ tān nābhi jāḥ smṛtāḥ ṣaṇṇavatyaḥ saha khāṇiśirāṇām hṛdi saṃsthitāḥ te vaiśivāni mārgāṇi viśvaḥ yatra pratiṣṭhitaḥ sarva nāḍīḥ parityajya brahmanāḍīm samāśrayet durgāṇi tārayet nauḥ iva arṇavam eka nāḍī nirālam vāta ālu madhye śiras gatā sānāḍī yoga yuktānām mokṣa dāsa ādi vaṃga tā majjā majjā vasā medaḥ kapham pittam śarīrayoḥ śirāṃsi tasya srotāṃsi ekaikam śukra randhrayoḥ hūta pāpa ādi vayānti mūrdhanibhitvātam īśvaram adhyāyaḥ devaiḥ sa divyaiḥ ṛṣayaḥ samagrāḥ brahmā ca viṣṇuḥ ca maheśvaraḥ ca vāyuḥ yamaḥ agniḥ varuṇaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ sarvān nirīkṣya eva divam prayānti mukha ābhimukhyaiḥ dhyāyaṃti gāyaṃti ca pūjayaṃti iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām ekonacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tathā ca oṃkāra devasya mahābhāgyam vadasva mama śṛṇu vyāsa paraṃgutyam rahasyam yogam uttamam tat param padam tat aham saṃpravakṣyāmi iyat mayā tu śrutam purā tīrtha upaniṣadam puṇyam mokṣa dam sarva dehinām kathayāmāsa deveśaḥ rahasyam jñānam uttamam sva puram citayāmāsa saḥ vimukta gaṇādhipaḥ vinā prāpya kutracid uvāca vākyam vara daḥ jagannātha pinākadhṛk yena kāryeṇa suśro śṛṇu siddhāntānām ca sarveṣām smṛtīnām ca eva suṃdari caturdaśānām bhuvanānām yaśva sāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ hi tat tat tat tat jñātvā mokṣam aśnute saḥ yaṃdevī sthitaḥ sākṣāt drāvāse svayam prabhuḥ tridhā sthānam tri bhoktāram tri bhojyam ca tathā aparam yatayā uśva param vidyāt sijyam te t bhāvam param āsthitāḥ om kāram paramam brahma paramam ca viduḥ budhāḥ pañca pañcan brahma samāyuktam pañca āyatana vāsinām ye drakṣyaṃti śivam tatra te drakṣyaṃti param padam brāhmaṇāḥ tava muñcati veda vedāṅga pāragāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ tava muñcati veda vedāṅga pāragāḥ yatayaḥ puṇya karmāṇaḥ ye ca anye veda saṃsthitāḥ nānā liṅga dhara vipra veda śāstra parāyaṇāḥ gṛhasthāḥ ca eva yatayaḥ tasmāt tīrthaupāsakāḥ ekadaṃḍāḥ tridaṃḍāḥ ca ye śaivāḥ pāśupata ayeca kapāla vrata cāriṇaḥ upāsate camām nityam mūkam ca vratam āsthitāḥ teṣām tu sarveṣām āsthitā iti aham śmaśānam taṃtra nityam sannihitā devaḥ jantūnām ca eva tārakaḥ tasyām puryāḥ vyavasthānāt prakhyātā amevimuktatā tathā saṃsāra bhīrubhiḥ tatra viśveśvaram dṛṣṭvā saṃsāreṇa patet punar viśveśvaram cakāram etad sāram prakīrtayet siddha kṣetram tapas kṣetram yathā vārāṇasī mune sparśana adarśanāt tasya kṛtārthā mānavā bhuvi tāraṇam sarva jantūnām nānā pāpasya nāśanam saṃdhyā upāsitā bhavati sakṛt vā adaśa māsakṛt patiḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām catvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ pūrṇabhadra sutaḥ śrīmān āsīt yakṣa pratāpavān tadā āsīta namaskāraḥ tad bhaktasya parāyaṇaḥ anuvrajan bhuṃjānaḥ uvā apidhāvan śva rūpam eva anuciṃtayan tasya evam yukta manasaḥ pūrṇabhadraḥ pitā bravīt kulīnānām evam vṛttiḥ bhavet suta vai svabhāvāt krūra cetasaḥ mahiṃsā śīlāḥ ca putrakaiḥ na eva kārya ānatā īvṛtiḥ evam dṛṣṭvā mahātmanām om namaḥ śivāya harikeśa ākhya guhmakaḥ daṇḍa pāṇiḥ abhūt deva pravam eva asati ananya bhāvena śaraṇam gacchati saḥ bhāva pradhānā pañcamī svayambhunā yathā dṛṣṭvā tyaktavan mahite bhavet māśrama antara jam karma na kuryāt gṛhinaḥ tatas deva tvam nodhi mārgeṣu mānuṣyam jātim eva ca na mayā vihitam tasya karma tat na atra saṃśayaḥ iti evam uktvā putraṃtu pūrṇabhadraḥ pratāpavān vārāṇasīm samāsādya tapaḥ tepe mahā ātmavān deṣaḥ śuṣka kāṣṭha upala upamaḥ tyaktvā gotra kṛtām vṛttim tathā ajāti kṛtāḥ tatas mahā āgatya ca dharma ātma a gokarṇa āyatane śubhe mārādhayan ye yogi īśam gokarṇa devam īśvaram saṃniyamya indriya grāmam avātiṣṭhata niścalaḥ sahasram ekam varṣāṇām divyam saṃnyativartata samākrāntaḥ bhakṣyamāṇaḥ pipīlakaiḥ rājasūcī mukhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ vidhyamānaḥ tathā eva ca bhaḥ etasmin antare devī vijñāpayati śaṃkaram udyānam punar eva idam draṣṭum icchā mita ivaraiḥ iti vijñāpitaḥ devaḥ pārvatyā parameśvaraḥ harvaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ yathānyāyam ākhyātum upacakrame nirjagāma ca deve śaḥ pārvatyā saha śaṃkaraḥ udyānam darśayāmāsa devyāḥ devaḥ pinākadhṛk vyajijñapat prajvāla nānā druma gulma śobhitam latā pratāna avanatam manoramam virūḍha puṣpaiḥ paritas sugandhitam su puṣpitaiḥ kam aśoka puṃnāga vanaiḥ su puṣpitaiḥ dvi repha mālā ākula saṃcayaiḥ kvacid kvacid praphulla ambuja reṇu bhūṣitaiḥ vihaṃgamaiḥ śvāru phala praṇādibhiḥ kvacid ca kāraṇḍa varāḥ vana āditam kvacid ca matta ali kula ākulīkṛtam mahā kalābhiḥ śraṃmara aṅganābhiḥ niṣevitam cāru sugandhi puṣpitam pragīta vidyādhara cāraṇam ca pravṛtta nṛtya anugata apsaras gaṇam prahṛṣṭa nānāvidha pakṣi sevitam pramatta hārīta kula upamoditam mṭaga indra nānā ākula mānasaiḥ kvacid gajaiḥ kvacid daddha kadamba kaṃmṭagaiḥ praphulla nānāvidha cāru paṅkajaiḥ saras taḍāgaiḥ upaśobhitam kvacid nibiḍa nicula nīlam nīlakaṇṭha abhivāsam mada mudita vihaṃga bāta nāda abhirāmam kusumita taru śākhā ālīna matta dvirephena iva kisalaya śākhā śobhitam prāñc śākham ta cāru vīrudham kvacid latā āliṅgita cāru vakṣam yadā viśāla alasa gāminībhiḥ niṣevitam kimpuruṣa aṅganābhiḥ pārāvata dhvani nikūjita cāru śṛṅgaiḥ akarṣaiḥ sita manohara cāru rūpaiḥ nīlaiḥ puṣpa stabaka tarala prānta darśitam deva śobhayā aparayā ayutam sadā vārāṇasī mama sarveṣām eva jantūnām hetuḥ mokṣasya sarvadā asmi siddhāḥ sadā devi madīyam tratam āśritāḥ nānā liṅga dharāḥ nityam mama loka abhikāṃkṣiṇaḥ abhyasyaṃti param yogam yukta ātmānaḥ jita iṃdriyāḥ nānā vasa samākīrṇe haga rājite kamala utpala puṣpa ādyaiḥ sarobhiḥ samalaṃkṛte tathā apsaras gaṇa gandharvaiḥ sadā saṃśobhite śubhe rocate mama sadā vāsaḥ yena kāryeṇa tat śṛṇu yathāmokṣam iha āpnoti brahma ādayaḥ vijānaṃti ye ca siddhāḥ mumukṣavaḥ na atas priyataram kṣetram tasmāt mama harate manaḥ mahā kṣetram idam tasmāt avimuktam iti smṛtam ha mattāḥ dṛṣṭa aśva anya puṣṭāḥ kokilāḥ yatra devyai prayāgāt api tīrtha agryāt idam eva mahat smṛtam jaigīṣavyaḥ sata siddhi yogāt sa mahā tapāḥ māhātmyam tat vakti āmama bhāvanāt jaigīṣavyaḥ mahā śreṣṭhaḥ yoginām jñānam icchati dhyāyata iti atra mām nityam yogāt nirvāpyate bhṛśam kaivalyam paramam yāti devānām api durlabham manaḥ ca eva sāyujyam īpsitam sthānam eva ca mahāyakṣaḥ tathā sarva arpita triyaḥ kṣetrasya vandanā deva gaṇeśa tvam avāpa ha parāśara sutaḥ yogī ṛṣiḥ vyāsaḥ mahā tapāḥ brahma āca ṛṣibhiḥ sārdham viṣṇuḥ vāyuḥ divākaraḥ upāsane mahātmānaḥ sarveṣām iha suvrate siddhāḥ channa rūpa ama ha vratāḥ alaṃkāra purīm enām mad prasādāt avāpsyasi tena evam pūrvatas kṛtvā catur varṇa samākulām sphīta aṃjanapada ākīrṇā abhūtvā ca vasatim naraḥ tatas prabhṛti cārvagiyeyekṣetra nivāsinaḥ gṛhiṇa āliṅginaḥ vāpi mad bhakta amad parāyaṇāḥ mad prasāda āgamiṣyanti māḥ kṣaṃ parama durlabham iha kṣetre mṭataḥ saḥ api saṃsāre na punar viśet ye punar vimama adhīrāḥ sattva stha avijita indriyāḥ sarvathā mama vibhāvitāḥ deha bhaṅgam samāsādya dhīmantaḥ saṅga varjitāḥ param mokṣam prasādāt mama suvratāḥ janma antara sahasreṣu yum jan yogī samāpnuyāt etat eva param jñānam etat eva param śivam atra āgata vividha duṣkṛta kāriṇaḥ api pāpa kṣayāt dirajasaḥ pratibhānti martyāḥ yasmin ṭatāḥ tanubhṛtaḥ padam āpnuvanti mūrkha āgamena rahi tān ahi saṃśayaḥ utra tare devāḥ devīm prāha girīṃdrajām tam prasādam yakṣāya vara bhaktāya bhāvitam magāma yakṣaḥ yatra āste kṛśaḥ dhamanisaṃtataḥ tam dṛṣṭvā praṇatam bhaktyā harikeśam vṛṣadhvajaḥ divyam cakṣuḥ adāt tasmai uvāca atha tathā ca enam varaiḥ dosmi iti coditaḥ itiśeṣaḥ udbhūma sambhramau karmaṇī iti ekacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ om anna da tvam ca lokānām gāṇapatyam tathā akṣayam avimukta vane sthānam paśyeyam sarvadā yadā bhaviṣyasi gaṇādhyakṣaḥ vara daḥ sarva pūjitaḥ jeyaśva api sarveṣām yoga aiśvarya samanvita anna daḥ ca api lokebhyaḥ kṣetrapālaḥ bhaviṣyasi tryakṣa śvadaṃḍa pāṇi śva mahāyogī tathā eva nirvāṇa bhairavam śaraṇyam devam īśānaiḥ moṃkāram śiva rūpiṇam devadevam mahādevam kaṇṭaṣadhvajam sadāśivam virūpākṣam śūla hastam jaṭā dharam kam sarva jantūnām namasyāmi namaḥ namaḥ vanhi bhāskara saṃkāśam sūrya koṭi sama prabham tu atra tu atra tadā ekadā oṃkāra nirdiṣṭa stotram śambhoḥ paṭhiṣyati avimukte mahā kṣetre sarvātmanā abhisaṃskṛtaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ śūdraḥ upi yadivā paṭhet veda aham etam puruṣam mahantam āditya varṇa tamasaḥ parastāt tam eva viditvā an abhavet mṛtyuḥ na anyaḥ pathī vidyatehi janānām tadā ca oṃkāra devasya śakyam māhātmyam īritum māhātmyam oṃkāra hata eka deśam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām oṃkāreśvaravarṇanam nāma dvicatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca natṛbhiḥ adhigacchāmi oṃkārasya kathām parām tām divyām paurāṇām veda saṃmitām śambhogiri mutā devī bhāryā kālī iti viśrutā tyartha dayitā sādhvī śīla vṛtta guṇa anvita sadā sadā upāste śaṃkaraḥ vaśī saṃdhyā pūrvā paścimān ca oṃkāre saṃsthitaḥ haraḥ nṛtyamānāḥ sthitāḥ sarve gīta vāditra saṃvṛtāḥ madhu śata varṣa sahasreṇa sveda bhūtā gaṇāḥ tathā ta bhūtāḥ tathā devāt sṛṣṭān anṛtuḥ uttamam padepade tam tādṛśam atho dṛṣṭvā gaurī vacanam abravīt kim virūpa akṣan nṛtyaḥ yaḥ mama vismaya kārakaḥ anekaiḥ bahuṣu sthānaiḥ dṛṣṭam nṛtyam mayā purā kailāsena eva saṃdṛṣṭam kadācid tu mayā purā kāraṇam katham yatu adya yadi anugraha bhāgaḥ tasmin sthāne oṃkāra āyatane svam gulena mahā tmanā metra sthāne girisute śṛṇu parikīrtitaḥ ayam idam brahma pañcāsyam saṃsthitam prabhum pañca pañca asthi pañca āyatana vāsinam tena nṛtyāmi aham devi parama ānandam āsthitaḥ brahmāṇḍa udara varti pañcāyatanam uttamam narāṇām anya buddhīnām viṣaya ākrāṃta cetasām tu saṃsthānam veda śāstra bahiṣkṛtāḥ hāṃta adānta ajita krodhāḥ pañcāyatana pūjayā sadbhāva bhāvitāḥ sarve drakṣyanti parameśvaram yaiḥ tu janma antare devi purā ārādhitā iti aham te vidanti param sthānam avimuktam param padaṃ brahmāṇḍa udara madhye ca yāni tīrthāni suvrate vārāṇasyām gamiṣyaṃti vaiśākhasya caturdaśīm drakṣaṃti paramam devam pañcāyatana vāsinam pūjayā a śama dama ādi sādhana saṃpannā bhavati iti āha om om namaḥ devāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ ca eva rudrāḥ pāśupata āśvaye parivārya sthitāḥ sarve oṃkāra īśam tu suvrate yasmin kṣetre svayambhu śru asthitaḥ pūrveṇa keśavaḥ rudrāṇām ca eva koṭiḥ tu kāśi purī eva saṃsthitā dhyāyamānā ca oṃkāra sthitā tasya eva dakṣiṇe vāmadevaḥ ca sāvarṇiḥ aghoraḥ kapilaḥ pare sapta koṭyaḥ tu mantrāṇām sarveṣām tapasā adhikaḥ evam madīyam śāśvatam śubham rakṣanti satatam pañcāyatana vāsinam rakṣanti satatam pañcāyatana vāsinam oṃkāra darśanāt eva gatim prāpnoti durlabhām iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām oṃkāranirṇayaḥ nāma trayaścatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ asmin sthāne purāvṛttam ha ekamanāḥ śṛṇu rathaṃtare purākalpe rājā āsīt puṣpavāhanaḥ nāmnā lokeṣu vikhyātaḥ tejasā sūrya saṃnibhaḥ tapasā tasya tuṣṭena devadevena śambhunā malam kāñcanam dattam yathā kāma gamam mune ca yatheṣṭam vicaran sadā kalpa ādau saptadvī peṣutasya puṣkara vāsinaḥ tasya na aśnātu tad dīpam puṣkaradvīpa mucyate tasmāt tam deva dānavāḥ nāmnā acalā vaṇyavatī babhūva sā a pārvatī ceṣṭatamā bhavasya tasya ātmajānām ayutam vabhūva dharma ātmanām agya dhanurdharāṇām saḥ api āgatam vīkṣya muni pravīram pracetasam vākyam idam babhāṣe mama adya pūjā jātā ca sarva viditā mama sundarī iyam bhāryā mad alpa tapasā eva su toṣitena dattam mad mām ambuja gṛhaṃcasu dhīra dhātrā yasmin praviṣṭam api koṭi śatam nṛpāṇām sa amātya kuñjara sthauva dhanāvatānām muniḥ api avocata bhava antaritām pṛthivīpate nanu niśamya kathām abhūt anāvṛṣṭiḥ atīva raudrā a kadācid āhāram avindatā bhramatā na kiṃcid āsāditam vanya phala ādi sadyas atha abhyapaśyat mahat ambuja āḍhyam sarovaram paṅka parīta rodhaḥ tad mūlya lābhāya puram samastam bhrāntam tadā aśeṣam abhūt tadānīm upaviṣṭaḥ tvam ekasmin sa bhāryā bhavatām a gaṇe rudra āvāse tu saṃsthāya tvayā rātrau mahā śrutiḥ tatra dṛṣṭaḥ tvayā devaḥ divya āśvaryaiḥ vibhūtimān paramam bahma deva gandharva kiṃnaraiḥ dhyāyamānaḥ param brahma oṃkāra ākhyam tu īśvaram tvayā adya avagatam sarva pañca āyatana darśanāt bhaktiḥ ca eva tadā jātā a sāpatyasya nareśvaraiḥ kim ebhiḥ kamalaiḥ kārya varaṃśaṃsuḥ alam kṛtaḥ niveditāḥ tathā puṣpāḥ pañcāyatana vāsine dīyamānam ca devāya suvarṇasya śatam param tu a mahātmanā prabhāte ca tvayā tasmin dṛṣṭaḥ śaṃsuḥ yadṛcchayā matvā tasmin āyatane sthitaḥ maṇā tena rāja indra iyam vyuṣṭiḥ te gatā sa bhavān lubdhakaḥ jātaḥ sa patnīkaḥ nareśvaraḥ puṣpa anukalpanāt tasmāt śaṃkarasya ca pūjanāt iyam vyuṣṭiḥ tathā jātā pañcāyatana pūjanāt oṃkāra īśvara māhātmyāt alpena tapasā nṛpaiḥ īśvaraḥ tasmāt rakṣaskha rāja indra puṣkara tvam mahī tale avimuktam samāsādya kārra śaraṇam traja prasādāt tasya devasya draṣṭāsi padam īśvaram iti uktaḥ satu rājāvaiḥ etena eva tu mahā ṛṣiṇā sarva gātraḥ tuharpāḥ viṣṭaḥ tam abravīt janmāntaram tvayā ākhyātam trahmaṇām kula vardhanaiḥ saṃsāre tvad samaiḥ saṅgaḥ puṇya bhārāt tu jāyate evam prasādya tam vipram rājā atu kṛta niścayaḥ sa patnīkaḥ jagāma āśu vārāṇasyām mahā mune śambhoḥ priyatame deśe pañcāyatana mukkiṃde dakṣiṇām mūrtim āsthāya om kāraḥ tatra saṃsthitaḥ durlabham ca para sthānam mānuṣaiḥ akṛtātmabhiḥ taiḥ akṛtātmabhiḥ akṛta sukṛta sambhāraiḥ rudra āvāsa iti vikhyātam puṇya dam sarva dehinām drakṣyāmi īśvaram devam yam dṛṣṭavan odbhavaḥ punar teṣām dṛśyam ca gamyam ca tat sthānam śaśimaulinaḥ tīrtham ca sthāpitam vyātra daitya dānava nāyakaiḥ antar dhyāna śataiḥ nityam pūjyate parameśvaraḥ tatra gatvā āturaḥ rājarṣiḥ paramam bhāvam āsthitaḥ dhayānaḥ deveśam pañcāyatanam īśvaram mata ākāram vinirnatya jñāna dīpena īśvaram dṛṣṭvā avāsatuḥ rājarṣiḥ oṃkāram paramam padam tena vyāptam idam viśvam girā iva paramātmanā tu yad darśanāt nara āloke vijñāna aiśvarya bhājanāḥ dānānām durlabham dānam vratānām durlabham param sarvatra durlabham sthānam iti āha bhagavant śivaḥ bhaktyā paramayā yuktā mahādevam viśanti ca pūjayiṣyaṃti ye tatra sarva bhāvena śaṃkaram vijñeyāḥ te gaṇābhadre mānuṣī prakṛti sthitāḥ tu teṣām ca eva tu sarveṣām oṃkāram prathamam smṛtam oṃkāra darśanāt devi sarvedṛṣṭān asaṃśayaḥ uvāca devi paśya idam udyānam nirmitam purā bṛṣadhvajaḥ deva udyānaṃ hi didṛkṣuḥ bhagavant tat samaṃtataḥ pūrvasmin tu asi ge bhāge devaḥ devyāḥ parātparaḥ udyānam darśayāmāsa nānā kiṃnara nāditam nānā vṛkṣa samākīrṇa nānā kusuma śobhitam nānā vṛkṣa samākīrṇa nānā pakṣi vināditam campaka aśoka puṃnāga priyaṅgu śata saṃkulam sarvatas sa tad udyānam āsādya devīm prāha jagatpatiḥ manorame pārijātaka khaṇḍāni tathā kalpadrumāṇi ca mama loke caye vṛkṣāḥ viṣṇu loke caye śubhe iyam vārāṇasī devī śiva lokam samāśritā tiṣṭhate lokeśaḥ brahmā kamala sambhavaḥ tatas sarvāḥ oṃkāram ca ādi mukti dam ūrdhvam goloka saṃsthānam gavām ghāsaḥ svayambhu aiḥ samāpatat tatas mayā ūrdhvatas dṛṣṭā agāvaḥ tāḥ somapa anugāḥ tatas tau īkṣitāḥ tatra bhīta amāvaḥ tadā abhavan tejasām amama nirdagdha ana eka varṇa amṛpā āditāḥ na eka varṇāḥ tathābhūtāḥ yat etāḥ prekṣita āmayā tam vaiśaraṇya tām gatvā amām eva loka mātaraḥ āśritāḥ saḥ mama āgatya soma uham ca puṇyam asya api darśanam atra āhma ṇa ānīya sthāpitaḥ parameṣṭhinā brahmaṇā ca api saṃgṛtya viṣṇunā āsthāpitaḥ punar tam dṛṣṭvā brahmanā viṣṇuḥ proktaḥ saṃvigna cetasā samānīta mām idam liṅgam sarve te deva kaṇṭakāḥ ha vyāghra rūpam samāsthāya nirdagdhāḥ tejasā mayā vyāghreśvaraḥ tatas khyātaḥ nityam tatra aham āsthitaḥ na punar durgatim yānti dṛṣṭvā imam vyāghram īśvaram tava ājñayā ambikā ica atra tasya idam kadama āsthitam nirvāṇa nāma vikhyātam sura asura namaskṛtam dṛṣṭvā imam manujaḥ satyam paśu pāśaiḥ vimucyate bhava xchasthānam idam tasmāt etat mama puṇya darśanam dṛṣṭvā tat arjanam śilam iti yādavaḥ ṛṣiṇām pataye nityam devānām pataye namaḥ devānām pataye ca eva yoginām pataye namaḥ vara dāya ca bhaktānām namaḥ sarvagatāya ca tanmātra iṃdriya bhūtānām vikārāṇām gaṇaiḥ saha prakṛtyāḥ pataye nityam pūjyāya apara gāmine ja īśvarāya namaḥ nityam yoga gamyāḥ yaḥ raṃhase saṃsāra utpatti nāśāya sarva kāma pradāya ca avaśyāya namaḥ nityam namaḥ bhasma aṅga dhāriṇe tri upāsarpata dīna ātmā avāta tāta iti saḥ vavīt tatas vāyuḥ tad ākāśe śilā ī prāhasatvaram mālaṃkāyana putraḥ teyāḥ saudevena śambhunā tasmāt nandī iti nāmnā ayam bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ na taḥsa vāyu vacanāt nam dinam pariṣasvaje gṛhītvā ca āśramam nītaḥ nandīśaḥ tuṣṭi vardhanaḥ cūḍā upanayana ādīni karmāṇi apicakāḥ raha kṛtvā ca adhyāpayāmāsa vedān sa aṅga padakramān āyurvedam dhanurvedam gāṃdharva śāstram uttamam jñānam ca eva sarvāṇi nimitta jñānam eva ca ca bhūta grāma cikitsām ca mātṝṇām caritam ca yat bhujaṃgānām ca sarveṣām yat kiṃcid pariceṣṭitam sat ācāram dharmaśāstram dṛṣṭvā śuciḥ adīna ātma aprī yavāganasūyakaḥ maṃsam anuprāptau śilādasya mahā ojasau tau abhyarcya yathānyāyam śilādaḥ su mahā tapāḥ tau ālakṣya sukha āsīnau āsane parama arcite tau sarva jantūnām sarva lāke carācare uvāca guṇa sapannaḥ same vaṃśa vivardhanaḥ samāḥ na āyata saṃtuṣṭaḥ putram nandinam acyutam tayoḥ pāde sva śirasā apātayaṃtam aniṃditam tau tu tasya āśirṣa devau prāyuktām dharma nitya tām guru śuśrūṣaṇe bhāvam lokān ca eva tathā akṣayān hilādaḥ tau tathā alakṣyaḥ āśiṣā devayoḥ tayoḥ maṃbhītaḥ saḥ pṛcchat ṛṣi sattamau uvāca tapas vantau ṛṣi satyau gati jñau sarva dehinām ūcatuḥ te eṣa tanayaḥ tāta aṣṭa āyūḥ dharmataḥ adya ārabhya aṣṭame varṣe jīvitum na bhaviṣyati tatas sa śoka saṃtaptaḥ nyapatat bhuvi duḥkhitaḥ kā kī vilalāpa ha svaram śrutvā su śubhaḥ kandamānam ca tam dṛṣṭvā pitaram duḥkhitam bhṛśam uvāca kena tvam tāta duḥkhena vepamānaḥ ca rodiṣi duḥkham te kutas dbhūtam jñātum icchāmi tattvāt uvāca putra tvam kila varṣeṇa jīvitam saṃprahāsyasi ūcatuḥ tādṛśam sarva tatas mām duḥkhaiḥ mā āviśat anyaṃhino caturvidhau natau anṛta bhāṣiṇaḥ tena aham putra śokena bhṛśam pīḍita mānasaḥ uvāca devaḥ vā dānavaḥ vā api yamaḥ vā api kadācana uvāca kiṃtapaḥ kim parijñā naṃkaḥ yogaḥ kaḥ samāśritaḥ tena tvam dāruṇam mṛtyum vañcayiṣyasi putrakaiḥ uvāca viyayā mahādevena nāthena mṛtyum jeṣyāmi nā anyathā drakṣyāmi śaṃkaram devam saḥ mama mṛtyum vijeṣyati uvāca mahādevaḥ purā a dṛṣṭaḥ labdhaḥ tvam mama yatas sutaḥ bhavān tu varṣeṇa ekena katham drakṣyati śaṃkaram mad putra śakyam kartu vṛṣadhvajāt mṛtyum vijeṣya si uvāca na ātatapasā devaḥ dṛśyatena ca vidyayā śuddhena manasā abhaktyā dṛśyate parameśvaraḥ aham eva ca jānāmi yena drakṣyāmi śaṃkaram tvayā avisṛṣṭaḥ gacchāmi acireṇa trilocanam draṣṭum tātana saṃdehaḥ visṛjasva sutantumām mataḥ na hiṃsā vāya yāte syāt iti tātaiḥ vrajāmi aham tiṣṭhatam vā āśayānam vā ādhāvantam patitam tathā sahasrāṇi yama koṭi śatāni ca abhidravanti saṃkruddhāḥ daṇḍa pāśa uyata āyudhāḥ yena drakṣyāmi tat aham eva jānāmi iti anvayaḥ iti daṇḍa pāśa ādīni udyatāni āyudhāni yaiḥ tathā uktāḥ tatra api na anyathā tāta bhayam tvam me kariṣyasi bhāva śuddhim sa mā āsthitaḥ drakṣyāmi iva raṃ nātham devam mṛtyu haram param na mṛtyu kālaḥ yāmyaḥ uvā kariṣyati mama vyathām tam evam vādinam matvā bruvāṇam śuddhayā girā tapāḥ praṇamya sa pituḥ pādau śirasā ca mahā yaśāḥ pradakṣiṇam samāvṛtya saṃpratastheti niśvitam namaskārya pituḥ pādau saḥ didṛkṣuḥ udāra dhīḥ dhyāyate manasā devam praṇata ārti haram haram iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām catuścatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ nirgataḥ atha tad ānandī jagāḥ ma saritām varām bhuvanām iti vikhyātām sarva loka sukha āvahām tām praviśya tatas dhīmān ekāgraḥ hradi saṃsthitaḥ majā jajā pasatadānandī rudra parama kāraṇam koṭiḥ ekā yadā japtā tadā devaḥ tutoṣa tat āgatya āha bhagavant gṛheśarvaḥ kapardadhṛk uvāca praṇataḥ bhūyas prayata ātmā tadā eva ha dvitīyām taptum icchāmi ṭiṃ parama kāraṇaiḥ jajāpa koṭi manyāṃtu rudram eva anuciṃtayan dvitīyāyām tatas kāṭau saṃpūrṇāya vṛṣadhvajaḥ anyān ca bhagavan koṭiṃṭatīyām api jāpitum uktvā jagāma deveśaḥ devyā saha mahā dyutiḥ tatas tṛtīyām tatra eva koṭim anyām jajāpa ha yuga anta āditya saṃkāśam tatas samabhavat dapuḥ taptām koṭau tṛtīyāyām ajvalat vidyayā saha sataṃkareṇa saṃgṛtya auddhṛtyaśirasā tathā maṃspṛśam śva agra hastena nandinam kāmam atravī tu uvāca japeyam kāṭim anyām japeyam kāṭim anyām yam yam hiraṇuṣe kāmam te tuṣṭāva parameśānam jarā śoka vināśanam namaḥ kāma aṅga nāśāya trailokya hananāya ca namaḥ kāla ugra daṇḍāya ugra daṇḍāya vai namaḥ namaḥ nīlaśikhaṇḍāya sahasra śirase namaḥ sarvatas pāṇi pādāya sarvatas akṣi mukhāya ca sarvatas śrutaye ca eva sarvam ādṛtya tiṣṭhate namaḥ candra arka netrāya yogīśāya ajitāya ca pinākapāṇaye ca eva śūla mudgara pāṇaye namaḥ triśūla hastāya ugra daṇḍa dharāya ca namaḥ deva adhipataye rudrāṇām pataye namaḥ ādityānām capataye vasūnām pataye namaḥ dhyāninā dhyāyamānā yad dhyānibhiḥ saṃstutāya ca mṛtyave kāladaṃḍāya yamāya ca mahātmane avitre sarva devānām dharma āyāne ka netriṇe umā ruva indra rūpāya tathā nārāyaṇāya ca lalāṭa aṃkita netrāya tata ūrdhva jananāya ca mṛtyu pāśa ugra hastāḥ ya nakṣatra āloka sūtriṇam sarva bhūtāya saṃjñāya sarva bhūta annukampine antarbhūta adhivāsāya prāṇinām jīvanāya ca vāce ca vāgmine ca eva sūkṣma āyatanave namaḥ tad sampāda kāya prāṇa sva rūpa ayavā namaḥ te apaśave nityam kṣetrajñāya viṭāya ca mahā bhāga kartre ca prajānām pataye namaḥ brāhmaṇāya viśuddhāya tathā durvāsase namaḥ śilpine śilpa nāśāya viduṣe viśvakarmaṇe tāpine bhūtāya bhūtanāthāya kūṣmāṇḍa pataye namaḥ avaśyāya api avadhyāya ajarāya amarāya ca akṣayāya avyayāya eva tathā apratihatāya ca sarveṣām tathā eva puṇya rūpiṇe sūkṣmebhyaḥ ca ati sūkṣmāya sarvagāḥ yamahātmane na na viṣṇu tvam na deva tvam na api indra tvam ca kāmaye icchāmi aham viśvanātha saṃsārāt vinivartanam draṣṭum icchāmi yogena eṣa me dīyatām varaḥ tvam nogatiḥ purā deva tvam vā anātha ayanam mahat tvayā a tyaktasya ca eva āste vināśaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ tām anyām gatim na paśyāmi paśyāmi ātyaṃtikam sukham paśyāmi sarva loka īśa saṃsāra mati dustaram pratīccha mām mahādevaḥ epa medīyatām varaḥ yā edam prātar utthāya paṭhet avimanāḥ naraḥ caturdaśyām viśeṣeṇa brāhmaṇaḥ uvāyatiḥ tathā yaḥ tu imam śṛṇuyāt nityam śrāvayet vā dvijottamaḥ mahīyate pūjām labhate iti pañcacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ om namaḥ śivāya nandīśa ghora tapasā asam saḥ aśvamedha phalam prāpya rudra loke mahīyate stavam pāpa praṇāśanam eṣa mantra japaḥ ca eva saṃsāra vinivartakaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām paṃcacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ pādayoḥ śirasā ānatam karābhyām sammukhābhyām tu saṃgṛtya bhuvane śvaraḥ uvāca jagantām nāthaḥ vacasā atoṣayan śvatam nirīkṣya gaṇapān sarvān mahādevaḥ avadat punar akṣayaḥ ca vyayaḥ ca evasa pitāsa suhṛd janaḥ ye saṃdṛṣṭāḥ snigdha bhāvam gata āśvaye mama iṣṭaḥ gaṇapaḥ ca eva mad vīryaḥ mad parākramaḥ mama pārśva gataḥ sadā mad rūpaḥ ca eva bhavitā mahā yoga bala anvi taḥ ṛddhi yuktam sahat dīpam kṣīrodam amṛta ākaram kuśeśaya mayīm mālām svayambhuḥ ā tmanaḥ śubhām rūpiṇe tayā amālayā ānandīya bhaukaṇṭha avasaktayā tryakṣaḥ daśa bhujaḥ śrīmān dvitīyā eva śaṃkaraḥ atyartha tapasā ātava bhāvitaḥ samantāt yojanam kṣetram divya siddhi pradāyakam siddha cāraṇa sam kīrṇam apsaras gaṇa sevitam siddha kṣetram param gutyam bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā yat kiṃcid kurute naraḥ śubham vā aśubham vā atra sarva bhavati bhasmasāt japamānasya ataulyam vai rudrāṇām tat bhaviṣyati tatas japyam śrutam vāri gṛhītvā āhāra nirmalam uktvā ānandībhavaḥ ceti visasarja mahā tapāḥ divyatas haṃsa kāraṇḍava ākīrṇa cakravāka upaśobhitā trī rūpa dhāriṇī ca eva prāñjaliḥ śirasā ānatā padma utpala dala ābhākṣī mahādevam upasthitā uvāca yasmāt yajña udakā devi pravṛttā tvam śubha ānane tasmāt yajña udakānām abhaviṣyasi sarit varā kuryāt śuciḥ prayata mānasaḥ mahādevaḥ nandīśvara patiḥ prabhuḥ sātam āghrāya śirasi pāṇibhyām parimārjatī putra premṇā abhiṣiñcantī srotobhiḥ tanu jaiḥ tathā reṇa devadevī nirīkṣatī tāni srotāṃsi trīṇi syāt śrotrebhyaḥ patitā nadī nandī trisrotaḥ saṃpuṇyatitaḥ tām anvavīkṣata nandī trisrotas yaḥ parama harṣitaḥ yasmāt upapraṇādena pravṛttā āsām ahānadī tasmāt śivenakām tau ai uvāca vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ mukuṭam ca dadau tasmai kuṇḍale vāṭata udbhave tam tathā abhyarcitam vyomni dṛṣṭvā ameya prabhākaram deva ūpi rājyebhiḥ ṣi can na nā daśa tata guṇam yasmāt suvarṇāt niḥsṛtya nadīyam saṃpravartate tat suvarṇodakā nāmnā mahādevaḥ abhyabhāṣata prabhā māvartata nadī puṇyā proktā jāmbūnadī tatas tat ca jāmbūnadam nāma jāpya īśvara samīpāt tat ca jāmbūnadam nāma jāpya īśvara samīpāt tam phalam eteṣām yajña udānam mahātmanām tat ca jambūnadam divyaṃdavam jāpyeśvaram cayaḥ tri rātra upoṣitaḥ gatvā a snātvā abhyarcya ca śūlinam brāhmaṇān tarpayitvā āca yatra tatra mṛtaḥ naraḥ nandīśvarasya anucaraḥ kṣīroda nilayaḥ bhavet nandīśvara samaḥ nityam yaḥ vyayaḥ same sadā asyāt guṇapaḥ variṣṭhaḥ tvayā asamaḥ kānta vapūḥ bhavet iti iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām nandīśvarotpattiḥ nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ devaḥ nandīśvaram devam ca abhiṣicya vibhūṣitam iti ṣaṭcatvāriśaḥ adhyāyaḥ manyase tathā eva ca sarveṣām iti deveśa nandī pu ca u mahātmanaḥ tatas saḥ bhagavant devaḥ sura siddha gaṇa arcitaḥ prāc mukhaḥ sa gaṇeśaḥ vaibhūtvāt devaḥ maheśvaraḥ ciṃtayāmāsa sa gaṇā nūrudrān ca diśi vāsinaḥ evam ciṃtita mātrāḥ te gaṇādhyakṣāḥ mudā anvitāḥ te sthitāḥ dakṣiṇām āśām paścimām uttarām tathā ca ūrdhvam adhas te tuśūla hasta aniṣaṅgiṇaḥ nīlakaṇṭha asita grīvāḥ śuddha prajvalana īkṣaṇṇāḥ samāgatāḥ tadā vyāsaye brahmāṃḍa āvaraṇāḥ pañca adhaurvyāt ayaḥ mune mapālī śaḥ viśoka śva śata netraḥ śatānilaḥ tad ananta rudrāḥ śata śas śata pādāḥ śata ānanāḥ saṃprāptāḥ sarva loka īśāḥ tān śṛṇuṣva mahā mune tatas karāla vadanaḥ bhṛkuṭī bhūpita ānanaḥ pañca yojana vistīrṇaḥ dīrghatas tādṛś eva ca tatas catvāri iva pāṇḍuraḥ vṛtaḥ koṭi śatena eva sadṛśāṇām mahātmanām mahā yoga bala anvitaḥ somavarṣa iti vikhyātaḥ koṭīratha samāvṛtaḥ tādṛśāṇām gaṇādhyakṣaḥ devasya ca sthita ugratas ambā śivaḥ mahākāyaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ mahā balaḥ yugānta anala saṃkāśaḥ sthitaḥ sthira yaśas balaḥ candramauliḥ mahākāśaḥ catu bahuḥ vilohitaḥ taiḥ śūla pāṇibhiḥ sa pārṣadaḥ yam rudrasya sarva asura su pūjitaḥ idam gaṇapa nāma apataḥpurāt madhu āsanī sva pāda ūharaḥ śuciḥ sahasra bāhu caraṇaḥ sahasra akṣaḥ sahasrapād tryakṣaḥ candra kṛta āpīḍaḥ śiras mālā vibhūṣitaḥ candramauliḥ mahākeśaḥ koṭiśas parivāritaḥ tatas parivṛtaḥ somaḥ ājagāma mahā balaḥ tatas param samīpe tam devadevam vara pradam mahā tejāḥ caturviṃśati lakṣaṇaiḥ tad bā durvyātta āsyaḥ mahādeva ardha vāhanaḥ karāla vadanaḥ ca eva śaṅku karṇaḥ mahā balaḥ asi pāṇiḥ mahā tejāḥ śata pādaḥ kṛśa udaraḥ ajaikapāda vikhyātaḥ vṛtaḥ koṭi śata enasaḥ balaḥ sarvatas vadanaḥ śrīmān sarvatas hava bāhura pādaśva aśanim dhārayan śubhām ha taiḥ tu koṭīnām aṣṭabhiḥ ca ātmanaḥ samaiḥ nikumbha eti vikhyātaḥ śatapādaḥ śatānanaḥ mahā āgata iti aparaḥ ca atra taḍitkeśaḥ mahā balaḥ daṇḍadhārī mahā cakraḥ śam kha kunda sama prabhaḥ tatas uparaḥ sahasreṇa koṭīnām gaṇapaiḥ ṭataḥ sarpa mālā sarpa mālā śatambiḥ śradā ājagāma mahā tapāḥ mahā teja viśrutaḥ su mahā dyutiḥ tathā anyaḥ ca candrāyudhaḥ mahātejāḥ cakrabāhuḥ kaṭā kaṭaḥ tad koṭi śataiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ vataḥ samanudhā vati śaṅkukarṇaḥ abhyayāt ca eva gaṇa koṭyā mahā balaḥ nandikaḥ ca eva daśabhiḥ piṅgākṣaḥ aṣṭabhiḥ eva ca aprasiddhaḥ tad eka pāda tvāt iti bhāvaḥ vajyam koṭīnām aṣṭabhiḥ aṣṭakaḥ kaṭākaṭaḥ tad nāmakaḥ vināyakaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā kūṣmāṇḍaḥ nāma viśrutaḥ dhūmrakeśaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ patākī daśabhiḥ tathā muktā uṣṭādaśabhiḥ śata pañcabhiḥ eva ca sahasra śīrṣaḥ ṣaṣ vigaṇa koṭi śataiḥ vṛtaḥ haḥ kumbhakarṇaḥ tathā aṣṭabhiḥ viśvabalaḥ sahasreṇa manuḥ tasyāḥ śatena vai tathā aṣṭabhiḥ samabhiḥ candravartanaḥ mahīdharaḥ sahasreṇa koṭinā aṃgaṇapaiḥ yutaḥ praṇava āditya mūrtiḥ vai koṭyā ca eva hiḥ kumbhaḥ ca pañcadaśabhiḥ tathā saṃkocāt paraḥ thā sama śiras gaṇaḥ mahābalaḥ ca daśabhiḥ apasmāra śva viśrutaḥ śvā api nāma ājagāmaha koṭīnām ca sahasrāṇām śataiḥ viṃśatibhiḥ vṛtaḥ parita śvetaḥ ca ājagmuḥ mahā yoga valāḥ nvitāḥ bhūta koṭi sahasreṇa pramathaiḥ koṭibhiḥ vṛtaḥ meghasaudāmanīnām anavatyā koṭibhiḥ vṛtaḥ prabhākaraḥ ca viṃśatyā ā vidyudbhiḥ tu mahā balaḥ mṛtyuḥ ca eva yamaḥ ca eva kālaḥ viṣadharaḥ tathā tathā ekaśṛṅga abhivikhyātaḥ tathā abhṛṃgiriṭi śvayaḥ ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ gaṇapāḥ ca mahā balāḥ mukhena vādyāni tathā vādayantaḥ mudā anvitāḥ rathaiḥ nāgaiḥ hayaiḥ ca eva ṛkṣa markaṭa vāhanāḥ ekīkṛtya tad ākāśaṃsa kiṃnaraiḥ mahā uragam bherī śaṅkha mṭadam gaiśva paṇava ānaka gomukhaiḥ bherī gambhīra sat nādaiḥ nānā ḍamaru ḍiṇḍimaiḥ ājagmuḥ yatra śaṃkaraḥ munibhiḥ vyāsa saṃsiddhaiḥ vṛtāḥ sarve samaṃtataḥ ṛgvedaḥ dakṣiṇe bhāge divya kuṇḍala bhūṣitaḥ mavet aśva nānā rūpa dharaḥ śubhaḥ sadā sa purāṇāni nānā rūpa dharāṇi ca devadevaḥ mahādevaḥ yajña rūpa dharaḥ śubhaḥ dṛṣṭvā nārāyaṇam devam mahādevaḥ bravīt tadā manasā agambhīrayā atantu sa devam loka bhāvanam hṛṇu viṣṇo vacomatyam yat dakṣyāmi sureśvara yat ite ca priyam kṛṣṇa abhiṣekam kuruṣva ame prahasya ca mahādevam tatas nārāyaṇaḥ bravīt vibho devānām api devaḥ tvam pramāṇam tu na saṃśayaḥ rāvata ārūḍhaḥ ājagāma śiva antikam vasubhiḥ mārutaiḥ ca eva prāṇi vāsān mahā balaiḥ te viśvakarma ādya vicitra dehāḥ viśveśam eka akṣaram avyayam ca iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe nandi upākhyāne saptacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ te gaṇa īśāḥ mahāsattvāḥ sarva deva īśvara īśvaram om namaḥ śivāya mad artha ca sama ājñaptāḥ ājñāpaya vacaḥ mama mad sāgarān śoṣayāmaḥ pāṭayāmaḥ su parvatān hanma etāḥ diśaḥ hanma etāḥ diśaḥ sarva ayamaṃvāsaha bāndhavaiḥ kasya adya vyasanam ghoram kariṣyāmaḥ te ājñayā tān tathāvādinaḥ sarvān satatam bhakta vatsalaḥ uvāca devaḥ saṃpūjya gaṇa andraḥ maheśvaraḥ śṛṇudhvam yatkṛte pūrvam iha āhūtāḥ a jagat hitāḥ mad ca praṇata ātmānaḥ kurudhvam tat aśaṃkitāḥ maṃdīśvaraḥ yaṃputraḥ naḥ sarveṣām īśvara īśvaraḥ priyaḥ gaṇāgraṇī devaiḥ kriyatām vacanāt mama saināpatya abhiṣiṃcadhvam mahā gaṇapati patim adya prabhṛti tvad mayam nandīśvaraḥ prabhuḥ evam ukte bhagavantā rudrāṇī gaṇakāḥ śubhāḥ meru saṃkāśam śubhaṃsam upakalpayan hātakumbha mayam ca api varam cāmīkara prabham muktā dāma nibham ca eva maṇi ratna vibhūṣitam stambhaiḥ vaiḍūrya mayaiḥ kiṅkiṇī jāla saṃkulam caturaṅgaka saṃyuktam maṇḍapam viśvatomukham tasmin saṃsthāpya deveśam abhyaṣiṃcan tanandinam ca eva mukuṭam hāram eva ca haraḥ ṛṣayaḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca enam pitāmaha purogamāḥ namaḥ kūṣmāṇḍa rāgāya vajja udyata karāya ca sālaṃkāyana putrāya halamārga utthitāya ca māṃśikā vaṃśa vādanam śīlam yeṣām goviṣāṇikāḥ rudra bhaktāya devāya namaḥ te jalaśāyine namaḥ gaṇādhipataye mahā yogi īśvarāya ca daṃḍaghaṃṭāya caṇḍāya ekādaśaśatāya ca akṣayāya amṛtāya eva ajarāya avyayāya ca paśūnām pataye ca eva rudra rūpa dharāya ca namaḥ prabala veśāya sarvajñāyāḥ jitāya ca tad kirīṭine kuṇḍaline mahā parigha bāhave prāñjaliḥ praṇataḥ bhūtvā jaya śabdam cakāra ha tatas sarvāṇi bhūtāni brahmā śakraḥ tathā eva ca ḍiṃḍima dhenukāḥ ca eva mardana aśva saha sraśas tatas śaṅkha aśru bherī aśva mardala aśva sahasraśas haṃśāḥ ca vāṃśikāḥ ca eva karkarā goviṣāṇikāḥ gaṇapāḥ sa yakṣa asura pannagāḥ namaḥ nandīśvarāya iti yaḥ kṛtvā stutim ācaret tasya kūṣmāṇḍarājebhyaḥ na bhavanti iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām nandīśvarābhiṣekaḥ nāma aṣṭācatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatas tān āga tān devān devānām adhipaḥ haraḥ mārutān prāha saṃgrātya kanyā artha sat patiḥ prabhuḥ mārutāvaḥ mahābhāga amahāsatvā mahaujasaḥ mantrya nāmnātān devān sarvān śakra purogamān om namaḥ vaḥ prīti dā kanyā subhagā divya rūpiṇī dātum arhatha tām śuddhām ūcuḥ yuṣmākam ca eva tasya tatas te punar eva īśam prāñcam kuḥ vākyam idam surāḥ śaktāḥ sahasram api aṃśam voḍhum na ca vayam bhavaiḥ kānaḥ śaktiḥ sura īśāna tejaḥ māheśvaram param draṣṭum dhārayitum vā api prasādam kurunaḥ saṃjagrasuḥ naṣṭa balān vinaṣṭān mahantaḥ saṃcchinna hārāḥ patitāḥ striyaḥ tāḥ hīnāḥ paraiḥ bhakṣayitum pravṛttāḥ karāla daṃṣṭra vikṛta ānanāḥ tāḥ tā bhakṣyamāṇāḥ patitāḥ taruṇyaḥ priyān sa roṣam vai eva pitāmahaḥ mad namaḥ śivāya yeṣu lokeṣu bhagavant saṃsthitaḥ girijāpatiḥ tad yakṛtaḥ yaḥ cakāla kṣaya āgataḥ tayoḥ bheda vikāra śṭaṇu vyāsa samāhitaḥ yoyama atheṣajas śabdanupeta vālakhilya purogāśva siddhāśva kāpila ādayaḥ mahā yogam pariprāptāḥ sattva ādi guṇa varjitāḥ te manīṣiṇām tapaḥ satyam dhṛtiḥ ca eva tapas vairāgyam eva ca ca atas paramparaḥ divye paramāṇoḥ pade sthitaḥ manasaḥ prākṛtasya ādau tat tejaḥ saṃprakāśanaḥ mahantaḥ sarvatas nityāḥ īśvarāt tat abhūt tadā tasmāt dijasya nirbhedaḥ kṣatrāt sa vibhuḥ smṛtaḥ bhūtā vaiṣṇavā pro ktā asau ca tasmāt vinirgatā amuṣya puratas brahma abrahmaṇaḥ śaṃkara ātmanaḥ yat sthānam vigraheśasya īśvarasya mahātmanaḥ tatra tatra vyāsaiḥ gatiḥ īśvara yoginām śatam śata sahasrāṇām yojanānām tat ucyate mahā maṇḍala saṃsthānam tad madhye vimalam śubham mahatā ajātarūpeṇa prākāreṇa sa veṣṭitaḥ śatam śata sahasrāṇām yojanānām yathādiśam divyā marāvatī bhūmiḥ sparśa mātra sukha āvahā ca mahā krada pramāṇa aninānā vaiḍūrya saṃnibhāḥ gandhavanti mahārhāni vinyastāni mahī tale mahā maṇi nibhāni ca mahā maṇi nibhāni ca kvacid kṛṣṇāni raktāni divya gandha vahāni ca taḥ pure bhagavantaḥ śambhoḥ parivārya nivodha tāḥ mahāpagā bahu tāni jala amṛtam na devān muni indra aśva na asurāḥ paśavaḥ na ca antarbhāva viśuddha āye sarvatas bhakti bhāvitāḥ meru śṛṅga pratīkāśaḥ dṛśyate ca punar punar prāsādaḥ ūna kṣapā ādiḥ tu kāma daḥ kanaka āmayaḥ a nirīkṣyaḥ mahā lubdhaiḥ samantāt pariśobhitaḥ vaiḍūrya vyoma saṃkāśaiḥ sphaṭikaiḥ candra saprabhaiḥ pravālaiḥ arka saṃkāśaiḥ indranīla mayaiḥ śubhaiḥ śikhiḥ asmi prakāśābhiḥ kvacid arka svarūpibhiḥ śobhita santu patākābhiḥ virarāja sukha anilam śuśubhe tat puram divyam pādapaiḥ kā mada aiśvitam yathā eva kāñcana meruḥ sarveṣām pravaraḥ mahān tatra viśveśvaraḥ sā kṣāt mahābhūta parigrahaḥ patyāṣaḍūiṃśaḥ sa parigrahaḥ lakṣmī medhādhṛtiḥ ca eva śrīḥ kīrtiśva sarasvatī umayā mahitāḥ tatra modate lokamātaraḥ tāḥ tā muni īśvarā divyā rūpinyaḥ yoga saṃyutāḥ gaṇānām adhipāḥ tatra kuna vāmana rūpiṇaḥ kāmarūpa a mahā veśa a mahā yoga parāyaṇāḥ pramathānām mahātmānaḥ tatra tiṣṭhaṃti suvratāḥ mahākāla īśvaraḥ tatra nandīśvara gaṇeśvarau paṭṭiśau divyau sadevau devapārśvagau devyāḥ pārśve sthite nityam asi haste mahā bale mahānādaḥ mahān nīśvaravāhanaḥ tatra āste megha saṃkāśaḥ gopatiḥ kāma rūpa dhṛk śākhaḥ caiva viśākhaḥ ca eva naigamī ca eva suvrata mārāśvasthitā pārśva loka anugraha hetavaḥ daśa sūrya sahasrāṇi rathe sūkṣme jagatpateḥ śārdūlāḥ kāñcanāḥ tatra siṃha aśva rajata prabhāḥ prājñānām maṇi tulyānām mahā yoga bala ojasām ttamaḥ sakala aṃkas gṛha īśasya de va deva jagat sṛjaḥ sarva bhāva arpita ātmānaḥ ye yogāḥ rudra tatparāḥ yatra tatra mṭatā vat sa teṣām tatra āspadam smṛtam te ye ca māheśvara āvyāsa tiṣṭhate śaṃkara ālaye anye ye śaṃkare bhaktāḥ tān śṛṇuṣva samāhi taḥ ahaṃsanandanaḥ ca eva sanaka śva sanātanaḥ dhātā brahmā āsatu jyeṣṭhaḥ nara nārāyaṇau api muniḥ hayaśiraḥ āyaśva yājñavalkya ādayaḥ tathā bhagavantaḥ śuka dharmāṇaḥ parama aiśvarya saṃyutāḥ tiṣṭhati īśvara mūla itu guṇa atītāḥ didṛkṣavaḥ te samāviśya prāpnuvaṃti āparāhnikam sya āyatanāni tu mahākāleśvaraḥ ca eva gokarṇa śva tathā aśubhau maheśvaraḥ ca deveśaḥ mahākāle ca śaṃkaraḥ bhadreśa śva mahādevaḥ śabdakarṇa īśvaraḥ tathā mahākāleśvaraḥ ca eva gokarṇe ca tathā śubhau avimukte ca oṃkāram yaiśvadṛṣṭam mahā mune kāle purā ca giri jāpateḥ yogaḥ pāśupataḥ yasya mayā ate parikīrtitaḥ bhaktiḥ yeṣām tyam kṛtārthāḥ te nara uttamāḥ mṛtāḥ śiva pure vyāsa bhikṣā paṭṭiśa pāṇayaḥ nandīśa skanda saṃkāśāḥ yoga aiśvarya bala anvitāḥ rudrāḥ bhavanti vipra indra sadā śaṃkara pārśva gāḥ sakalam ca eva jñātvā evam vijñāya parameśvaram bhaviṣya sica yogīca jñānasya asya prabhāvāt jñāna sitdhyā smṛtim prāpya brahmāṇḍa udbhava kāraṇe sthiti dharma nirodhānām vijñāna artham anusmṛtya caturdhā vikariṣyasi tvad kṛtāḥ prakariṣyanti tīrthakṛt tvam bhaviṣyasi tasmāt ratam ca saṃprāpya paśu pāśa vimocanam śaṃkara jñāna saṃpanna īśvara ilayam āpsyasi tad kṣaṇāt ca asya yogā usau prādurbhūtaḥ mahā muneḥ abhivādya guruṃcyāsaḥ brahma putram mahā tapāḥ sava āyatena dīkṣā artham viveśa ca mahī talam evam sanatkumāraḥ tu pṛṣṭaḥ vyāsena dhīmatā muni indra kathayāmāsa purāṇam śiva sambhavam śiva yoga dharam dhīram sarva jñāna arṇavam mahat tasmāt yūyam api prāpya vratam pāśu patan dvijāḥ dyutiḥ purāṇam prathamam prāha ślāghyam nandīśvara uddi jaḥ kṛtsnasya jagantaḥ vidyāsu ādi kartā yathā haraḥ tathā sarva purāṇānām purāṇaḥ yaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ mṛtyu kālam anuprāpya nate śocanti janminaḥ śravaṇāt devadevasya sāyujyam dhāḥ raṇāt vibhoḥ ślāghyāt puṇyam umāpateḥ hi jagantām stotra anuvādam param mama bhāva arpita sarva bhāva hṛdaya yaiḥ yaiḥ yam sevitaḥ sarve te jvalat arka vanhi vapuṣa ru yakṣāḥ śaśāṅka tviṣaḥ devasya anucarāḥ catu daśa vara a nirmukta sarva aśubhāḥ sarve harṣa samanvitāḥ śruta dhiyaḥ nānā guṇaiḥ anvitāḥ tataiḥ eha paramam prāpya yogam muni indrāḥ parama parama nantam prāpya deva adhivāsam tripura haram imam ye jñātavantaḥ prayatnāt gata kaluṣa cayāḥ te prāpnuvate ca mokṣam idam purāṇam paramam pavitram śuciḥ paṭhet yaḥ śṛṇuyāt ca yaḥ naraḥ pitṝṇām pitṝṇām paṭhyamānam idam bhavet duṣṭa svapna ādi duṣkarma kali kalmaṣa nāśanam ślokam śloka arthā eva āsa māhitaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitāyām saptapaṃcāśattamaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptā iyam saṃhitā bhāvanā eka vaśam devam bhavānī sahitam bhavam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe sanatkumārasaṃhitā samāptā
